Current Commentary

From the Nineteenth to the Twenty-First Day 31

The League of Nations special assembly, planned for this year on March 3rd, was convened due to the increasingly deteriorating situation in the Far East and the difficulty in mediating between China and Japan. On March 11th, it resolved Article 3, based on Article 15, Paragraph 9 of the Covenant. According to China's request, in order to comprehensively handle the Sino-Japanese dispute, it would proceed with the "conciliation method" stipulated in Article 15, Paragraph 3 of the Covenant, and apply the "recommendation procedure" stipulated in Paragraph 4 of the same article. Therefore, the Committee of Nineteen was established, its purpose being: "First, to stop the acts of war; second, to pay attention to the League of Nations Council's resolution of September 30, 1931, that Japanese troops should withdraw to within the railway zone, to reiterate the resolution of September 30th on December 10th, and to dispatch an investigation team to the Northeast; third, to resolve the dispute as soon as possible and strive to create a draft agreement; fourth, if necessary, to propose to the Assembly to seek the opinion of the International Court of Justice; fifth, to prepare a final report based on Article 15, Paragraph 4; sixth, to consider proposing emergency measures when necessary; seventh, to submit the first progress report to the Assembly in the near future (no later than May 1, 1932); eighth, all obligations to create documents and report to the Assembly must require the Assembly to notify the Committee." At that time, our representative Yan expressed silence because the instructions from our country had not arrived, while the Japanese representative Matsudaira declared abstention. The resolution was still passed unanimously with 45 votes.

Since this spring, the situation of the Sino-Japanese dispute has not only not eased but has become increasingly worse. Direct negotiations are impossible, and the report of the League of Nations investigation team is still awaiting confirmation, dragging on until today. The League of Nations Council meeting, from its opening on November 21st to its closing, produced no resolutions other than the war of words between the representatives of China and Japan. After one round of discussions by the Committee of Nineteen, it was handed over to the Assembly. In the Assembly, the representatives of Ireland, Spain, Czechoslovakia, and Sweden proposed "Please deny that the September 18th Incident was an act of self-defense by Japan and declare that the creation of 'Manchukuo' was the result of the presence of Japanese troops..." This is indeed a theory that explores the root cause and a key to Far Eastern peace. The suggestion to include the United States and Russia in the Committee is particularly important.

×　　　　×　　　　×　　　　×

In the past two days, most of the speakers at the League of Nations Assembly were from small countries, all of whom were able to set aside [blank space] to maintain peace. British Foreign Secretary Simon's speech stated that "the Manchurian problem has many unique features, and restoring the old state of affairs in the Northeast is an impossible solution. Sino-Japanese disputes should emphasize practicality and not ideals..." This newspaper's daily commentary yesterday already considered this judgment to be insufficient in its understanding. It has detailed our views on the unique features of the Manchurian problem, the restoration of the old state of affairs, practicality versus ideals, and direct negotiations, clarifying the hopes of our people. It is a fact known to the world that "Manchuria is Chinese territory, forcibly seized and occupied by Japanese military force," and "the two most powerful elements constituting Manchukuo are the presence of Japanese troops and the activities of Japanese officials." The Lytton Report has already recorded this clearly. Why does Foreign Secretary Simon ignore it and not mention it? Moreover, the occurrence of the September 18th Incident was actually a premeditated act by Japan. The Second Division of the Multiple Gate and the Twentieth Division of the Chamber, the former far away in Sendai, Japan, and the latter in Yongsan, Korea, were able to appear between Taoyang and Changchun on the night of September 18th to fight. The Lytton Report also stated, "The Japanese side had a precise preparatory plan... The Chinese side, in accordance with its instructions, did not attack the Japanese army and had no specific time or place to endanger the lives and property of Japanese residents... The military actions of the Japanese side that night cannot be regarded as a legitimate means of self-defense." Sir Lytton paid attention and listed them one by one in the report. Is Foreign Secretary Simon so forgetful? Is this what he means by emphasizing facts? Furthermore, who is it that has provoked today's dangerous phenomenon, brought about the future crisis in the Far East, broken the "equal opportunity," and implemented market monopoly? Can there be anything more "practical" than the fact that the three northeastern provinces are now devastated and thirty million people have become fish and meat, and that the League of Nations Covenant, the Pact of Paris, the Nine-Power Treaty, and all resolutions of the League of Nations have been torn up under the Japanese bayonet?

If Japan continues to exert its resources, utilize the impulse of national enthusiasm, and rely on its past financial and commercial relations with Southeast Asia and India, and even use its naval violence to dominate Shanghai, attack Hong Kong, and extend as far as Singapore, what will happen? Therefore, for the sake of the friendship between China and Britain and the maintenance of permanent peace in East Asia, we hope that British Foreign Secretary Simon will carefully consider this Sino-Japanese dispute again, and refrain from making one-sided claims to avoid leaving a century of harm to the world and causing more serious consequences.

×　　　　×　　　　×　　　　×

Although the four-nation proposal did not advocate using force to restrain the atrocities of Japanese militarism, it had a clear understanding of the September 18th Incident as an act of aggression and "Manchukuo" as a puppet state. The nineteen countries of the Committee of Nineteen, including Britain, France, Italy, Germany, Spain, Portugal, Ireland, Guatemala, Mexico, Norway, Panama, Poland, Czechoslovakia, Colombia, Belgium, Hungary, Sweden, Switzerland, and Errmo, either because they were far across the ocean or because they lacked the strength to do so, had the heart to advocate justice and maintain fairness, but lacked the power to restrain atrocities. Moreover, the United States of North America, which has interests in the Far East, and the Soviet Union, which is closely related to the Northeast, are both standing outside the League of Nations, allowing Japan to use its diplomatic magic to pursue its policy of aggression between anti-Russian and pro-Russian sentiments, seizing our country's land and seizing the world market, surpassing the German Empire before 1914. The United States is now preoccupied with its own affairs and has difficulty confronting Japan alone, while the Soviet Union is meticulously building its own country and still maintains its tradition of "ironic observation." All of this indirectly benefits the monopolistic imperialism of Japan and dares to pose a huge threat to international peace.

Foreign Secretary Simon truly lacks a correct understanding of the facts of the Shenyang Incident and the current situation, which we deeply regret. However, since he theoretically recognizes that "the League of Nations Covenant is our constitution, we cannot freely discard it, and we must try to maintain it and find a practical solution..." then Foreign Secretary Simon has never failed to uphold the League of Nations and has never failed to seek a solution quickly. Now that Japan has relied on its military force to discard international covenants and tear up all treaties since September 18th of last year, is there any "practical solution" other than using force to restrain Japan? As for the Committee of Nineteen adding the United States and Russia to become twenty-one countries and becoming a truly international cooperative mechanism, although it may not be able to immediately restrain Japan's actual effects, will peaceful mediation be more powerful?

The League of Nations Assembly ended perfunctorily, and the Sino-Japanese case was transferred back to the Committee of Nineteen to handle, with a deadline to submit a draft resolution in the shortest possible time.

The Candidate for Acting Chairman of the Committee of Nineteen is Undecided, the Assembly Passes the Appointment of Avenol as Secretary-General 32

(Geneva) The League of Nations Assembly today did not make any concrete decisions regarding the Sino-Japanese dispute this afternoon and adjourned temporarily. The draft resolution proposed by small countries condemning Japan's policy of aggression was ultimately not passed due to the major powers siding with Japan. The Assembly only resolved to transfer the Lytton Report and all relevant opinions to the Committee of Nineteen, which will convene as soon as possible to formulate recommendations and report to the Assembly. This resolution by the Assembly is clearly beneficial to Japan. The entire practical issue of the Sino-Japanese dispute has deviated due to the strategy implemented by Japan, leading to the issue of international interference in China's reconstruction efforts. At this time, the situation of the League of Nations is indeed worse for China than it was in March of this year. Some even recognize Japan as a loyal member of the League of Nations, while China's current situation has become the object of discussion. The major powers, especially Britain and France, seem to be leaning towards Japan. In the face of the current unfavorable international situation, China has no way out other than self-help. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 9th)

(Geneva) At 2:51 PM today, the League of Nations Assembly continued its meeting. Chairman Hymans declared that the main staff of the Assembly had already met and deliberated, and now presented the following resolution:

The Assembly has received the report of the Commission of Inquiry established in accordance with the Council resolution of December 10, 1931, the opinions of both parties, and the records of the Council meetings from November 21 to November 28 of this year. The Assembly, also taking into account the discussions held at the Assembly from December 6 to December 9 of this year, now requests the establishment of a special committee in accordance with the resolution of March 11 of this year. Its duties are: 1. To study the report of the Commission of Inquiry, the opinions of both parties, and the opinions expressed by the Assembly, and to submit recommendations to the Assembly in any form; 2. To draft proposals in order to resolve the dispute submitted to the Assembly in accordance with the Council resolution of February 9 of this year; 3. To submit these proposals to the Assembly at the earliest possible time.

Chairman Hymans stated that since there were no objections, the proposal could be established and said that since this proposal had been passed, all documents and suggestions related to this dispute must be transferred to the Committee of Nineteen, asking it to work as quickly as possible. The Committee has the freedom of action and discussion and will be convened as soon as possible.

Hymans then proposed the appointment of the French national Avenol as Secretary-General, requesting the Assembly to approve it. A vote was held immediately, and Avenol was elected with 42 votes out of 43. Those present praised the retiring Secretary-General Drummond. The Chairman then announced that the work of the Assembly was temporarily suspended and that the next Assembly meeting would be announced later and would be of a non-public nature, followed by a public meeting of the Council.

It is widely believed that the Committee of Nineteen will meet on Monday. However, Chairman Hymans cannot attend due to Belgian political reasons. The issue of electing an acting chairman arose today. Some advocated electing the Swiss representative Motta to act as chairman during Hymans' absence, but this proposal was opposed because Motta spoke vehemently at the Assembly meeting. Currently, the Italian representative seems to have the best chance of being elected as acting chairman.

When the Committee of Nineteen convenes on Monday, Chiang Kai-shek is determined to invite the United States and Russia to participate in the mediation work. The Committee will adjourn after holding another meeting and will reconvene after Christmas. (Reuters dispatch on the 9th)

(Geneva) The Assembly staff held a secret meeting at 10:05 this morning, attended by Chairman Hymans, British Foreign Secretary Simon, German Foreign Minister Neurath, Swiss President Motta, Spanish representative Madariaga, French Foreign Minister Pongou, Irish representative Connolly, and Italian representative Aloisi. They did not encounter any difficulties in deciding on the future procedures, because Hymans had already agreed with Japanese representative Sato on the procedural issues proposed by Matsuoka last night. The four-nation proposal will be transferred to the Committee of Nineteen together. It was subsequently decided to transfer all proposals and speeches to the Committee of Nineteen without any instructions. The meeting adjourned at 11:10.

(Geneva) It is reported that Britain has now re-emerged to lead the countries, seeking a feasible solution to the Sino-Japanese dispute. Simon is planning to convene the Committee of Nineteen on Monday to quickly draft a document inviting the United States and Russia to participate in the mediation work and submit it to the League of Nations Assembly for approval, and then immediately send it to Washington and Moscow. It is reported that Chairman Hymans has not yet decided on the date for convening the first meeting of the Committee of Nineteen. (Kuomintang dispatch on the 9th)

Guo Taiqi Solemnly Declares Rejection of Direct Sino-Japanese Negotiations

Agrees to Invite the United States and Russia to Participate in the Discussion of the Manchurian Issue, Any Solution Must Be Based on the Provisions of the Covenant and Treaties 33

(Geneva) At the continuation of the League of Nations Assembly on the afternoon of the 8th, Chinese representative Guo Taiqi rose to speak after the representative of Colombia, Quijano. First, he explained China's position [Government position is consolidated, boycott is legal, self-defense] stating that the boycott and the activities of the volunteer army are legitimate self-defense plans and will continue. The National Government is now quite stable and its power is growing. The Lytton Report has statements regarding this matter, and the London Times and the Shanghai North-China Daily News have also confirmed his statement, which can be verified. Guo then read out the report and the articles from the two newspapers mentioned above.

[Firmly rejects direct negotiations, agrees to collective negotiations] Guo then reiterated the reasons for China's firm rejection of direct negotiations with Japan but stated that China is prepared to agree to the conference proposed by Sir Simon within the League of Nations, including both the United States and Russia. This conference must be based on the League of Nations resolution of March 11 of this year and Section 3 of Chapter 9 of the Lytton Report, which states "Any solution must comply with the provisions of the League of Nations Covenant, the Pact of Paris, and the Nine-Power Treaty." China also insists that the troops must be withdrawn in accordance with the resolution of March 11 before the meeting can be held. China is loyal to the League of Nations and is determined to handle the Sino-Japanese issue within the scope of the League of Nations regulations from beginning to end.

[Different Sino-Japanese policies, vastly different British and Japanese behavior] Guo compared the policies set by China for Asia with the policies set by Japanese soldiers, asking the audience to pay attention. Guo stated that what the Japanese call "Manchukuo" is actually a deception and insult to the world by Japan. On Tuesday, Japanese representative Matsuoka proposed a basic point, asking whether any member of the League of Nations was prepared to support the League of Nations to forcibly impose a solution. Matsuoka asked this question with threatening words, but he (Guo) would never ask this question with threatening intent. This is a fundamental question that must be answered. Even the spokesmen of Japanese militarism could not change world opinion during the Shanghai negotiations. He personally deeply believes in the great power of the League of Nations Assembly. Guo also said that the British behavior in Shanghai has some reasons, because large-scale military actions may endanger foreign concessions, but the Japanese have no such reason, and the British have not engaged in aerial bombardment or artillery bombardment. The Japanese speculative ventures in China are vastly different from British behavior. To claim that British behavior has become a precedent for British behavior is actually slandering civilized Britain.

[Japanese currency plummets, economic strength is limited] Guo also spoke about China's resistance, stating that the boycott and armed resistance will never diminish, and the volunteer army is determined to fight to the end. China has greater support than Japan, which cannot afford the burden of taxes and military expenses. Guo then asked the audience to pay attention to the fact that the current Japanese currency has decreased to two-fifths compared to last year and stated that no country in the world can be isolated in spirit, politics, and economy for a long time. A week ago, the two-day debate at the Council meeting had already caused various stock prices in the Tokyo market to fall by five to seven pounds sterling. Matsuoka's statement that China is not an organized country and therefore the League of Nations Covenant does not apply to it was seemingly agreed upon by the Canadian representative. The Lytton Report has already refuted it, and to say that the Chinese government can allow Chinese land to be divided is completely nonsensical.

[Vows not to recognize the puppet state and will not succumb to force] Guo then solemnly said, I can tell the Assembly, and tell Japan, that we will never recognize the so-called "Manchukuo," and we will never allow the land of the three northeastern provinces to be seized or the thirty million people of the three northeastern provinces to be reduced to slavery. I think that there is not a single person in any country represented in the Assembly who would not say this. Guo stated the reasons why the boycott is an absolutely legitimate self-defense, stating that last year, many highly responsible citizens in the United States formally proposed to join China's plan to boycott Japan. Guo also stated that before September 18 of last year, Japan used major international unpleasant events as an excuse. At that time, the Chinese government was willing to submit the dispute to arbitration, asking the League of Nations or other arbitration organizations to adjudicate the disputed points, but Japan refused and resorted to force. The method of the League of Nations has not been tried by Japan.

[Faithfully fulfills the Covenant, not responsible for anything] But China has adopted all methods within its power. Japan's invasion of the three northeastern provinces is a rare event in modern history. However, China still abides by the obligations of the League of Nations Covenant and the Pact of Paris and faithfully fulfills the Council's advice not to take any actions that would aggravate the situation. These records can all be verified. Anyone with a fair mind cannot condemn China and Japan as being equally responsible. China has had faults in the past, and China is still prepared to submit to the court. But in the current situation encountered by the League of Nations, China bears no responsibility whatsoever.

[Forcibly occupies vast land, what is it if not aggression] Guo also stated that Japan has no treaty rights to station troops in the railway zone before the September 18th Incident of last year. But there is one thing that is more important than illegally stationing troops in the railway zone, that is, the problem of forcibly occupying thousands of miles of vast land outside the railway zone. To say that this is by no means a large-scale military aggression is a fallacy.

[Withdrawal of troops is a prerequisite, welcomes US and Russian participation] The future actions of the League of Nations Assembly must be based on the utmost respect for the principles set in the Assembly resolution of March 11.

Its basis and scope, before the start of negotiations, there is an indispensable condition, that is, the occupation by the Japanese army must end. Yesterday, Sir Simon said that he had briefly heard about direct negotiations. If Sir Simon had any concerns, then it was not heard from the Chinese representative. China is unwilling to negotiate directly with Japan. If anyone holds the opinion that China and Japan can negotiate directly, then this opinion should be dismissed. But the League of Nations Assembly can rely on China to do its best to assist. Although China opposes direct negotiations, it supports collective negotiations handled by the League of Nations. China believes that the best mechanism to handle this matter is none other than the Committee of Nineteen assisted by the United States and

Turn to page 7

Page 7

Russia. Guo most [blank space] summarizes China's attitude: China is prepared to negotiate a solution, but the negotiations must be collective in nature and handled by the Committee of Nineteen. Before the negotiations begin, the Assembly should pass a resolution declaring that the members of the League of Nations do not recognize "Manchukuo" or have relations with it.

During the negotiations, they must be based on and restricted by the principles contained in the resolution of March 11 and Chapter 9 of the Lytton Report. The Assembly should take the judgment of the Lytton Investigation Team as its own judgment and declare that the maintenance of Manchukuo is contrary to international obligations, so no member of the League of Nations may recognize it or have relations with it. Without this declaration, the negotiations will not be able to produce results. (Reuters dispatch on the 8th)

Matsuoka's Forceful and Unreasonable Arguments 34

Japanese representative Matsuoka continued his report, reserving the right to criticize the speeches made at the Assembly in the future, saying that he did not wish to elaborate at present, but that the previous speaker had taken phrases from the Lytton Report as the basis for opposing Japan's arguments, without reading the entire text, which was extremely unfair.

(The Lytton Report is Self-Contradictory) Although the report stated that the Japanese military's actions on September 18 last year were not a legitimate self-defense plan, another section of the report stated that the investigation team did not completely dismiss the assumption of related Japanese military officers that their actions were self-defense. He heard that some members of the investigation team would not acknowledge the former section without attaching the latter section. If the Assembly wished to obtain evidence, he could prepare to invite the investigators to attend the meeting for explanation. To add a crime to Japan and then make Japan prove its innocence was extremely unfair. The previous representative's remarks were completely based on misunderstanding. He reserved the right to speak later regarding Guo Taiqi's remarks about Japan's situation. In reality, Japan was suffering in the wave of world panic, just like other countries.

(Japan Only Has Soldiers, Not Warlords) Japan indeed has soldiers, but no warlords. Those such as Baron Tanaka, who had been Prime Minister, all came from humble origins, and could be taken as examples. The Japanese representative had already answered more than half of the points raised by the representatives, so he asked the Assembly to study Japan's written opinions. The Japanese military's presence in Manchuria was based on treaties to protect the lives and property of Japanese people. Manchuria had one million Japanese subjects. The United States had also sent troops to Nicaragua to protect the lives and property of American residents. Matsuoka then mentioned Simon's statement that neither side recognized the entire Lytton Report, saying that he wished to add to Simon's remarks that Japan saw in the Lytton Report a report of agreement amidst disagreement. Anyone with clear eyes could see the self-contradictory text. The investigation team's achievement of "agreement amidst disagreement" or "disagreement amidst agreement" proved that they each possessed a conscience, but the self-contradictory nature of the report made it impossible for Japan to fully accept it.

(Deep Regret for Joining the League of Nations Initially) The Italian representative Aloisi said that the League of Nations Covenant had flexibility. He deeply agreed with this statement. If this was not taken into account, any action by the League of Nations would contradict the principles of the League of Nations. Japan had initially decided to join the League of Nations in Versailles, initially believing that the United States would also join, but the United States ultimately decided not to join. When the United States decided not to join, Japan's selfish viewpoint also argued that Japan should not join. However, Japan ultimately decided to join because Japan sincerely wished to contribute to the work of the League of Nations. Today, many people in Japan feel that Japan's situation has not been understood by the League of Nations and want to withdraw from the League of Nations.

(Struggling for Life, Not Warmongering) Japan is encountering a serious situation in China and a terrible situation in East Asia. Japan is currently only struggling to preserve the overall situation, not to create war. Soviet Russia has not joined the League of Nations, so the League of Nations must have some flexibility and must not act as if countries such as Russia and the United States have already joined the League of Nations. Several speakers at the Assembly referred to the League of Nations as the lifeline of their existence. Japan refers to Manchuria as Japan's lifeline. However, when the speakers referred to the League of Nations as their lifeline, they were speaking out of selfish interests. "Manchukuo" can continue to develop steadily and will eventually become the cornerstone of peace in the Far East.

(Parading Three Puppet Representatives) The Assembly should know the facts about Manchukuo. There are currently three people in Geneva who are related to "Manchukuo," such as Edward, the former Chief Inspector of the Chinese Maritime Customs Service, who has been appointed as an advisor to "Manchukuo." All the people of Japan are united behind the government to express their opinions and support the government's actions in Manchuria. The 65 million people of Japan are united as one to support these actions. Can you say that these people are all crazy? This is truly absurd. The reason why the Japanese people are united is that they believe that the entire survival of Japan, the life and death of Japan, depends on this issue. Even with the most severe judgment under the League of Nations Covenant, Japan is prepared to resist it.

(Actually Claiming to be the Savior of China) China violated the Otsu Treaty and began to increase its influence in Korea. Moreover, the greatest cause of the Russo-Japanese War was the secret anti-Japanese alliance between China and Russia. If Japan had not defeated Russia, would there still be China today? At that time, Japan saved all of China, and when the Chinese leaders took refuge in Japan, Japan also saved the entire Republic of China. If we accept and withdraw the Manchurian troops, the first thing to decide is who can restore order. China may demand this sovereignty, but who will command these troops? Zhang Xueliang's troops or someone else's troops? But the Lytton Report has already stated that the status quo cannot be restored. I fear that the people will suffer for several more years as a result. The report states that China must have a strong central government, but how can a strong government be obtained?

(Has a Compromise Really Been Reached Between Russia and Japan?) Six months ago, no Japanese newspapers advocated concluding a non-aggression treaty with Russia, but today, the majority of newspapers are vigorously advocating concluding such a treaty because Russia recognizes Japan's position in Manchuria and does not want to interfere. Once you give the Chinese people hope that they can obtain foreign assistance, you will not achieve peace in the Far East for a single day. Soviet Russia understands this truth. By preventing countries from joining any side, the League of Nations has made a great contribution in the Far East.

(Again Attempting to Fabricate Our National Opinion) However, China still clings to the idea that the League of Nations will help China to restrain Japan. We know that many people in China want to understand Japan, but dare not express their opinions publicly for fear of being attacked and put to death. Some people in Europe and America believe that world opinion opposes Japan and that Japan is resisting the world's sentiments. As far as we know, public opinion is gradually leaning towards Japan.

(Pretentiously Comparing Japan to Jesus) He then continued, saying that world opinion opposes Japan, but didn't Jesus, a thousand years ago, get crucified by world opinion? If Japan is being judged on the cross today, public opinion will soon turn to Japan as well.

(Falsely Accusing Us of Being Red to Divert Attention) Today, the spread of Red Communism in central China is four times the land area of Japan. Once Japan's position is weakened, Red Communism will extend to the mouth of the Yangtze River and spread to a greater part of China. If the League of Nations' desire for world peace and Far Eastern peace is sincere, then the consolidation of Japan's position is the only tool to realize the League of Nations' hopes, he said.

After Matsuoka finished speaking, Chairman Hymans declared that the main staff of the Assembly would meet at 10:00 a.m. the next day to consider the two draft resolutions and Matsuoka's request that the four-nation draft proposal be immediately put to a vote or immediately withdrawn. It was heard that the main staff would first consider the proposal put forward by Switzerland and Czechoslovakia to ask the 19-member special committee to study the matter and submit its resolution to the Assembly.

The meeting was scheduled to resume at 2:30 p.m. the following day. (Reuters, 8th)

Outline for Reorganizing Party Affairs in the Bandit Suppression Area

Headquarters Formulates and Promulgates 42

(Hankou) The headquarters formulated the "Outline for Reorganizing Party Affairs in the Bandit Suppression Area" and promulgated it by order on the 9th. The main points are that, except for the provincial and special municipal party departments, the county party departments will have one secretary and one assistant, who will be selected from among those with positions. The expenses of the party department should be saved as much as possible. The necessary party fees should be donated by the party members and should not be paid by the provincial and county treasuries, in order to set an example of party members relying on the party. Each county party department should have 500 party members. If there are not enough, two counties will be combined into one party department. (Special Dispatch, 9th)

Britain Prepares to Pay Expiring War Debts in Cash and Asks the United States to Hold a Debt Meeting

The Paris Conference Decides on the Attitudes of Britain and France; the US Replies to the Second French Note 55

▲ Reuters, London, 8th: The atmosphere here is filled with talk that Britain will pay its debts due on December 15, and that French Prime Minister Herriot will also advise France to pay its due interest. However, there has been no official criticism. It is believed that Herriot will soon send another note to the United States asking to hold a debt meeting.

▲ Reuters, London, 9th: British Prime Minister MacDonald left Paris for Geneva last night and is expected to return to London this week, at which time he will immediately hold a cabinet meeting to draft another letter to the United States. Roughly, Britain will state in this letter that it will repay its debts in cash and express its satisfaction with the United States' statement that it is prepared to investigate the debt issue, but urge the United States to begin the investigation as soon as possible.

Contents of the US Reply to the British Note 56

▲ Reuters, London, 8th: Regarding Britain's request to postpone payment of its USD 95.5 million debt to the US due on December 15, the United States has replied, which in effect amounts to a denial. The reply stated that the US President is prepared to cooperate with the British government through any appropriate agency to study the overall situation and consider methods to restore the stability of currency and exchange rates, revitalize trade, and promote prosperity. The United States welcomes close study of this matter by the US and Britain to prepare for the recommendations of the World Economic Conference, but this does not imply the cancellation of debts. In order to consider other forms of repayment with a view to expanding the US market for exports, it is necessary to conduct this study. In the view of the United States, the foreign debt problem is closely related to disarmament. The United States cannot agree with Britain's statement that US war debts were used entirely for destructive purposes, and that the repayment of these war debts has resulted in the collapse of world commerce and the concentration of large amounts of cash in the United States, and that the complete cancellation of war debts is necessary for world recovery. A large amount of US debt was indeed used to purchase non-destructive goods and was resold to others, and some of the US debt was used to maintain the exchange rates of the Allied countries outside the United States. The United States believes that Britain has overstated the impact of debt repayment on world recovery. As for the so-called debt repayment having exhausted the gold reserves of the debtor countries, there does not appear to be any factual evidence of this. The United States does not recognize the statement that the Lausanne Agreement was tacitly approved and endorsed by the United States. The US Congress appears to be able to approve a method of depositing gold pounds in London, which, at the appropriate time, would be remitted to the United States at the guaranteed US dollar price. However, it is heard that Britain is unwilling to follow this method because the impact on the foreign exchange market of a large number of British pounds awaiting remittance to the United States is no less severe than purchasing foreign exchange. The US government is deeply convinced that Congress can consider any reasonable method that facilitates the payment of the installment due on November 15.

▲ The US Reply to the French Note is Sent 57

▲ Reuters, Washington, 8th: The United States' reply to France's request to postpone payment of the December installment of its debt was delivered to the French embassy today.

▲ National Press Agency, Paris, 9th: The French parliament has scheduled a debate on the war debt issue for Sunday. French Prime Minister Herriot is expected to seek a compromise solution in the next few days that will not offend the United States and will not force France to pay. However, French newspapers predict that this win-win solution will be difficult to achieve. It is said that Herriot will suggest to the US government that the issue be submitted to the International Court of Arbitration in The Hague to delay the matter, but it is feared that the US government may not agree.

Results of the Paris Conference 58

▲ Reuters, Paris, 8th: The meeting on war debts lasted four and a half hours and adjourned at 2:35 p.m. A communique was then issued stating that the British and French governments considered the status of the Lausanne Agreement and studied the difficulties arising from the repayment of debts on December 15. Although both countries retained the right to take individual action to deal with the matter, they both declared their common determination to seek international cooperation to promote world economic recovery. According to responsible sources, Britain will repay its next installment of debt to the US in gold bars. British Prime Minister MacDonald is scheduled to return to Geneva tonight, and Chamberlain will return to London.

The Democratic Party's Asian Policy (Part 1) 65

The Tokyo Mainichi Shimbun published on the 2nd of this month a lengthy article by Lieutenant General Sato Kiyokatsu entitled "The Change of U.S. President and its Asian Policy," detailing the future diplomatic policy of the United States and the inevitability of war with Japan. Readers of this article will understand the changes in the future international situation, and the conflict between Japan and the United States is not far off. We have translated it as follows:

㈠ Changes in Economic Policy

Since the victory of the Democratic Party's Roosevelt in the U.S. presidential election on November 8th, people in our country (Japan), both in the government and among the public, have believed that the Asian policy of the Republican government will inevitably change, and the tense diplomatic relations between Japan and the United States can be eased. In reality, the diplomatic policy of the United States is unlikely to change simply because of a change of president. Tracing back to the U.S. Republican Party, it is based on imperialistic policies, leaning towards capitalists; the Democratic Party advocates liberal policies, focusing on farmers and laborers. Since the European War, the imperialistic characteristics of the United States have become increasingly pronounced, and the Republican Party has frequently won elections, such as Harding, Coolidge, and Hoover (all of whom came from the Republican Party), who abused their imperialistic diplomacy. Among those most affected was our Japan, such as the return of Qingdao and other interests in Shandong to China, forcing our Japan to sign the Nine-Power Treaty, destroying the Anglo-Japanese Alliance, and restricting the tonnage of the Japanese Navy, etc. Our country (Japan) has been constrained everywhere. However, today, due to its own economic panic, the United States, in order to protect capitalists, has raised tariff barriers; in order to develop economic hegemony, it has caused instability in European debts; in order to achieve mass production of capital supremacy, it has blocked its sales channels. As a result, millions of people in the country have lost their jobs, and the bankruptcies of banks and companies have occurred one after another. All of these are caused by the policies of the Republican Party. Now, the economic policy of the Democratic Party is to reverse this tragic economic phenomenon, and it has won the election victory. However, it is not known that the difference in opinion between the economic policies of the Republican and Democratic parties is that the Republican Party adopts protectionist trade, while the Democratic Party adopts free trade, much like the differences in opinion between the Conservative Party and the Liberal Party in Britain. Therefore, after the Democratic Party's Roosevelt ascended to the political stage, he will only ease the protectionist policies that favor capitalists and implement free trade.

㈡ The Open Door Policy

Although the economic policy of the Democratic Party has changed, will its foreign policy also change accordingly? This is what we should pay the most attention to. Originally, the foreign policy of the United States has always had far-reaching goals, attempting to achieve a grand plan for a hundred years, so it cannot change its original direction due to changes in the political situation. If we try to view it from the perspective of modern American history, we can understand its content. Therefore, we are talking about the Democratic Party coming to power, thinking that it can change the United States' Asian policy, which is truly a lack of understanding of the world's trends. The current Asian policy adopted by the United States has far-reaching goals and is deeply rooted. The United States originally has vast territory and abundant resources, but how to maintain its prosperity and well-being forever is a major problem. Therefore, since the end of the last century, enlightened people in the United States have believed that the only way to solve this problem is to seek a large market in the world. However, although Canada and South America have vast areas, their populations are sparse, and they have always welcomed British goods. Most of Africa is a British colony, and the population is extremely small. Its eastern neighbor, India, although it has a population of 300 million, is also a British colony, as is Australia. As for the European countries, they all have their own industries to supply their own consumption. The United States knows this, and the only way to develop foreign trade is to develop towards Asia. The elderly China in Asia has a population of 400 million, and everything must be supplied from overseas. The United States considers it to be its only customer. Therefore, in 1899, Secretary of State John Hay declared the Asian policy of the United States. The U.S. government has inherited this policy to solve domestic and foreign problems. (To be continued)

Page 9

Record of the Chengdu Street Fighting Catastrophe

Prosperous City Streets Turned to Scorched Earth, Cultural Institutions Completely Destroyed, Student Deaths Exceed a Thousand 66

Chongqing News - Chengdu is the capital of Sichuan Province, with an area of nine li and three fen, and a population of approximately 300,000. It is the cultural and political center of Western Sichuan, with wealth and bustling markets that surpass the entire province. Since the unprecedented massacre by the roving bandit Zhang Xianzhong at the end of the Ming Dynasty, it has gradually prospered over the past 300 years. In the past, when Sichuan Army's Liu Cunhou drove out Guizhou Army's Luo Peijin, there was a street fight. At that time, it was only in the Fucheng area in the center of the city, and the result was that Fucheng, which had a history of several hundred years, was transformed into a field of rubble, which has not yet been restored to its original state. Unexpectedly, during this Sichuan war, the 29th Army and the 24th Army actually waged war in the provincial capital. The intensity of the disaster and the depth of the damage not only far surpassed the Luo-Liu war but could be traced back to the tragedy of Zhang Xianzhong. The city was in ruins, and the dead were everywhere. It was truly a catastrophe unseen in 300 years. I previously wrote about the losses suffered by the people of Sichuan in the war, but Chengdu was only briefly mentioned because news was blocked at that time, and most of the information was obtained from rumors. Now that the street fighting has stopped, and postal and telecommunications have been restored, details are easier to obtain. Therefore, I am specially supplementing the account to serve as "Shu Bi" [Sichuan History] viewing.

(Street Fighting Lasted a Week)

The 29th Army and the 24th Army were locked in a stalemate in Chengdu for more than a month. Initially, Tian Songyao still intended to wait and see. When the 21st Army captured Luzhou, and Li Yang advanced and occupied Zizhong and Jianyang, he began to send troops to attack Liu Wenhui, resulting in street fighting. From the early morning of November 16th, the fighting lasted until the 24th. The Tian and Liu armies engaged in hand-to-hand combat 73 times. Initially, it was limited to the city, but later it spread to various areas attached to the city. The battle line stretched for more than 50 li. On the side of the 29th Army, 8 regimental commanders, more than 60 battalion commanders, more than 300 company and platoon leaders, and more than 5,400 soldiers died. On the side of the 24th Army, 9 regimental commanders, more than 40 battalion commanders, more than 400 company and platoon leaders, and more than 7,800 soldiers died. On the side of the 28th Army, some maintained neutrality, and some participated in the 29th Army's operations. 1 brigade commander, 2 regimental commanders, 1 battalion commander, 5 company and platoon leaders, and more than 800 soldiers died. As a result, more than 15,000 people from the Liu, Tian, and Deng armies died.

(More than 10,000 Civilians Died)

As for the civilian population, the Xinhua Street area (the gathering place for Chengdu prostitutes) became a battlefield. About 6,000 prostitutes died from stray bullets. In the area outside the city walls, more than 3,000 civilians died. Inside the city, except for Xinhua Street, more than 6,000 people died from stray bullets, including more than 1,500 students. Sichuan University, the highest academic institution in Sichuan and the cultural hub of southwestern China (formed by the merger of Sichuan University, Chengdu University, and Normal University), in the imperial city, had all its colleges, libraries, instrument rooms, etc., completely destroyed. A total of more than 500 male and female students of Sichuan University died. In total, more than 10,000 innocent people died, and about 40,000 houses were burned down by artillery fire and demolished by the army. The once-prosperous Dongda Street and the bustling Chunxi Road have now become fields of rubble. Businesses are scattered, and the streets are piled with stones. The tragic situation is unbearable to witness. At least the Sichuan Education Hall, Sichuan Library, Museum, Zoo, etc., on the side of the imperial city have also been reduced to flat ground. The culture of Sichuan and the antiques of hundreds of years have been completely destroyed.

(Newspapers Suspended Publication)

The 24th Army's newspaper, "Chuan Bao," published three large sheets a day and was quite influential. When the street fighting broke out, it was destroyed by the 29th Army. The 29th Army's newspapers, "National Daily News," "National Gazette," and "Current Affairs Weekly," etc., were also destroyed by the 24th Army. As for the other newspapers, either the editors were killed by stray bullets, or the responsible persons disappeared, making it impossible to publish. Only one or two newspapers began to publish after the street fighting completely stopped, but they did not dare to report on the street fighting situation. It was not until Tian Songyao and Liu Wenhui formally made peace, and Tian gave up Chengdu and the arsenal, that the situation in Chengdu gradually eased. At that time, the City Chamber of Commerce and gentry members initiated the organization of the Renshen Year Relief Society, established eight shelters to accommodate refugees whose houses had been destroyed, providing temporary accommodation, and established 24 porridge and cake factories to relieve the unemployed victims in the war zone, barely prolonging their lives. However, although the recent street fighting in Chengdu has completely stopped, and Tian Songyao has withdrawn from Chengdu, the defensive fortifications built in the streets and alleys have not only not been removed by the 24th Army but have also issued notices prohibiting destruction, and the engineering factory has been ordered to step up the production of weapons and make strict arrangements. Under these circumstances, Chengdu is likely to face a second major war. (December 7th)

▲National News Agency, Berlin, 8th - Communist radio broadcasts have recently been discovered frequently in the Berlin skies, followed by wild singing of The Internationale. The police have been diligently investigating for two weeks. Today, thanks to the effectiveness of scientific instruments, they were finally able to detect that the radio station was located somewhere in the suburbs of Berlin. The people in the room were already dismantling the radio equipment, preparing to transport it to another location, and a car was waiting outside the door to depart. Three people were arrested at the time, and it is said that many more were involved. From now on, the Berlin skies can be a little quieter.

The Key to the Sichuan Situation Lies with Deng Xihou

Liu Wenhui Makes Every Effort to Court Deng, Deng Plays a Pivotal Role in Both Sides, Allied Generals Urge Deng to Clarify His Attitude 68

Chongqing News - The long-pending Sichuan War is sometimes fierce and sometimes缓和，sometimes the two sides remain unmoved, and sometimes they draw their swords. Although the central government has issued a clear order to cease the war, and 70 million people in Sichuan are calling for peace, the giants ultimately ignore them like the autumn wind. Recently, in the Southern Route, the 21st Army and the 24th Army are locked in a stalemate in Jiading, with no progress. As for the war situation, in Renshou, the 21st Army is gradually advancing, and the 24th Army is gradually retreating. In the Central Route Longquanyi, Li Qixiang and Yang Sen are fiercely attacking the Liu army in the province because Tian Songyao is urging them to provide assistance, and fierce fighting has already occurred. Longquanyi is a barrier to Chengdu, only 60 li away from Chengdu. If Longquanyi is lost, Chengdu will be indefensible. Therefore, Liu Wenhui sent heavy troops to guard it, and it will be difficult to capture for a while. As for the 29th Army, which was defeated and retreated to the Xindu and Jintang areas, it has been urgently seeking to counterattack Chengdu to avenge the shame of its defeat. However, the Allied forces have not yet provided assistance, so they are still holding their troops. Liu Wenhui of the 24th Army, surrounded on all sides, is concentrating all the troops stationed in Xikang, such as the Hai Brigade, and other troops, in Jiading and Chengdu. Even if there is a warning that the Tibetan army is invading Xikang, Liu will find it difficult to cope with it. He is now prepared to fight the Allied forces with all his strength and determine the final victory or defeat. If defeated, he has indicated that he will hand over the entire 24th Army to Deng Xihou and travel alone. As for Deng Xihou's attitude, he is still unusually smooth. Deng originally sided with the Allied forces. When Tian Songyao led his troops to attack Liu Wenhui, he maintained neutrality on one hand, and on the other hand, he allowed his subordinates to join the 29th Army to attack Liu. When Tian was defeated, Deng took the position of mediator, playing his clever tricks and shifting the blame to his subordinates. Although Liu Wenhui knew this, he could do nothing. He could only express his goodwill to Deng and ask for his cooperation. On the one hand, he also hinted to his subordinates to repeatedly send telegrams to Deng, expressing support. Therefore, Deng did not turn against Liu. Currently, he has no clear indication to any party. However, the Allied forces believe that Deng's ambiguous attitude has a significant impact. If Deng cooperates with Liu Wenhui, he will inevitably call for the unity of the Bao faction and win over Tian Songyao. Although Tian and Liu Wenhui have a grudge, in view of their common interests, they have no choice but to cooperate temporarily. In this way, the strength of the three armies is no less than 200,000. If they launch a concerted attack on the Allied forces, it will be difficult to cope with. Therefore, on the 4th of this month, the generals of the 21st Army, 20th Army, Sichuan-Shaanxi Army, Li Jiayu, Luo Zezhou, and 29th Army sent a telegram to Deng Xihou, urging him to clarify his attitude as soon as possible. However, Deng has not yet made a clear indication. (December 7th)

Guangdong Plane Practice Crash

Pilot Killed, Squad Leader Slightly Injured, Cause of Accident Due to Engine Failure 69

Guangzhou Correspondence - The Guangdong Provincial Air Force, after establishing an examination committee to test the pilots of each team, immediately engaged in screening. After the screening, the Air Force Department sent instructors to actively train the pilots for days, teaching them wartime techniques, so that the Air Force Training Team could be established as soon as possible. At 9:00 a.m. on the 2nd of this month, according to the daily routine, a plane took off into the sky again from the Air Force airfield, engaged in practicing various combat maneuvers. The plane was named Albatross No. 6. The two people on board were the pilot of the Fourth Squadron, Zhong Runxiang, and the squad leader, Lu Yuheng, who was sitting in the back, directing Zhong to practice tactics. After taking off from the Shaogou airfield, they flew from south to north, about 3,000 feet above the ground, circled for a week, and then turned south, making a low-altitude bombing posture. When descending to a height of 300 feet, they felt a strange sound from the engine. They planned to land for repairs, but when the engine was raised again, the movement was as before. Thinking that the engine was in good condition, they no longer paid attention to it. From then on, they flew back and forth, performing various combat techniques. After flying in the sky for about half an hour, at 9:35, the Albatross No. 6 plane suddenly lost its slow movement and fell straight down from a height of 200 feet into a business in the northwest corner of the airfield. The pilot Zhong, in the front seat, bore the brunt of the impact. Squad Leader Lu was also thrown out, but only suffered abrasions to his lips and face and was still able to move. After the accident, Air Force personnel rushed to rescue Zhong and Lu. However, Zhong died on the spot due to his serious injuries. It was found that Zhong graduated from the second term of the Aviation School and was currently a lieutenant pilot in the Fourth Squadron, 23 years old, from Guanshanxu, Nanhai County. The captain of the Fourth Squadron, Xie Mang, immediately sent him to the coffin company due to his death, and telegraphed the relatives of the deceased to come and see the coffin, and planned to provide preferential treatment according to the example of those who died in the line of duty. As for the squad leader Lu Yuheng, who was involved in the same accident, because his injuries were very minor, he has returned to work as usual. After inspecting the cause of the damage to the plane, it was found that it was due to oil accumulation in the engine, which burned the electric bulb, stopped the power, and affected the entire plane, resulting in the crash. (November 3rd)

The Truth About the Mengcheng Drug Manufacturing Case

Key Criminal Chen Zaigong Has Been Escorted to Bengbu, But Li Mingxun Is Still on the Run 70

Bengbu Correspondence - The key criminal Chen Zaigong in the case of the evil gentry manufacturing heroin in Mengcheng County, northern Anhui, has been escorted to the Bengbu for interrogation. It has been found that Mengcheng is located in a remote area of northern Anhui, and the people have always been known for their strength. Qing Nian bandit Miao Peilin came from this place. The power of local evil forces has always been strong. The county and the nearby counties of Suhao and others are the most prosperous areas for opium production. Therefore, the spread of opium is even more widespread than in central Anhui. Although the authorities have repeatedly stepped up the ban, it is related to opium seedling tax revenue, and it has been impossible to eradicate it for many years. Li Mingxun, chairman of the Mengcheng County Chamber of Commerce (namely Li Ge), has been domineering in the countryside for a long time, and has been eyed by the people of the county. Li took northern Anhui as a source of opium, and the local price was relatively low. He had a whimsical idea, raised funds to set up an institution, specializing in the purchase of opium and the manufacture of heroin, in order to obtain huge profits. The drug manufacturing institution was secretly borrowed by Li Defa, the owner of the Defa grain store in Hebei, the county, and Zhao Baoyu and Zhao Huairen were responsible for the formulation. It is said that there were also two foreigners inside who served as main technicians. There were many shareholders, including Chen Xiuzhai, Gao Yishan, Wang Huaibao, and Yu Yiting. The car worker Wang Ziqing was solely responsible for transporting the soil. The four technicians mostly manufactured the drug manufacturing institution at night. The drug manufacturing institution was first set up inside the Defa grain store, and then returned to Li Mingxun's home and Chen Zaigong's home to manufacture secretly. The sound of the machine reached the outdoors. Li and others had three specially made double-bottomed boats, specializing in transporting drugs out of the country. Sometimes they loaded wheat on top and drugs underneath, first escorted by Yu Yiting to Bengbu, and then tried to transport them to Shanghai for sale. They made huge profits each time. Since the opening, they have made a profit of more than 100,000 yuan, which has been divided equally among the shareholders according to their shares. In September of this year, Yu transported 84 packages of heroin to Bengbu. The boat was parked on the river, and it was discovered by the military police inspection office of the garrison headquarters. Yu Yiting escaped, and the boatman Xie Kai was captured. At that time, Xie confessed everything, claiming that the drugs were mainly manufactured by Li Mingxun. At that time, the garrison commander Jiang Dingwen reported the news and sent personnel to Mengcheng for secret investigation. Li Mingxun temporarily avoided the wind. Last month, Jiang resigned from his post as garrison commander, and Xu Tingyao, commander of the Fourth Division, was ordered to take over. Mengcheng party members and educators Zhang Dong and Wang Jianhu filed complaints with the National Government, the Anhui Provincial Government, and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek then telegraphed Xu Tingyao to investigate. After receiving the order, Xu sent military judge Jin Shuo and 16 soldiers to Mengcheng to arrest the key criminals a few days ago. At that time, Li Mingxun fled again after hearing the news. Chen Zaigong was arrested. At that time, more than a thousand people gathered to intercede, but Jin refused. He handed Chen over to the Mengcheng County Government for detention and ordered him to be escorted to Bengbu for interrogation within five days. County Magistrate Qin Liangzao sent a team on the sixth to escort Chen in a car to Bengbu and handed him over to the military law department of the Fourth Division for custody. On the seventh, Xu Tingyao, together with Wu Baoming, director of the military law department, summoned him for interrogation. According to Chen, he only said that Li Mingxun manufactured heroin, but Li had fled to Anqing, and denied that he participated. After the interrogation, he was returned to the military law department for custody. It is said that he will be retried within days. Xu Tingyao is collecting evidence and has asked the military and political party authorities to issue an order to arrest Li and other criminals and bring them to justice. Chen Zaigong has been accused of many murders in Mengcheng. The family members of the victims, such as the wife of Ruzai, are now in Bengbu and have filed a complaint with the garrison headquarters, requesting that they be punished according to law. However, many Meng gentry have come to Bengbu to run errands for Li and Chen, hoping to ease the atmosphere. It is not known how this case will be resolved. (December 8th)

The Truth About the Bandit Areas in Western Anhui Counties

Report on the Anqing Inspection Group's Visit to Wuhu 72

Wuhu Correspondence: After the Central Army routed the Communist bandits in various counties of western Anhui, the Anqing provincial capital's party, government, and various sectors specially organized an inspection group for the bandit areas of western Anhui to inspect the bandit areas of Huoshan, Lu'an, and other counties. They arrived in Wuhu yesterday (the 6th). Today, they convened representatives from party, government, business, and various organizations at the county chamber of commerce to report on the situation they observed in the bandit areas. After an introductory speech by Wang Zuxun, a committee member of the Kuomintang party department, Wang Chun and Wang Zhensheng, representatives of the group, successively reported, stating that the main reasons for this inspection were: 1) to understand the true situation of the disaster in the bandit areas; 2) to widely publicize the situation in the bandit areas to the outside world; 3) to hope that leaders from all walks of life would jointly promote and provide spiritual and material assistance. As for the Communist Party's occupation of western Anhui, there were three reasons: (A) Poor politics: local officials and the self-defense corps abused their power, making the people easily susceptible to the Communist Party's enticements; (B) Cultural backwardness: the people's thinking seemed untouched by the times. For example, they suspected that automobiles were animals and asked how much rice straw they needed to eat each day; (C) Geographical relations: Lu'an and other counties had towering mountains and continuous ranges, allowing bandits such as Little White Wolf and others to occupy the mountains and dominate, harassing the people everywhere, which was then exploited by the Communist bandits. Due to these three major reasons, the people of western Anhui could not avoid this great calamity. However, after the Communist Party occupied western Anhui, they established a fake Soviet government in Zhufushan, Huoshan, and a fake Northwest District in Mapu Town, Lu'an, dividing the entire population into farmers, workers, and merchants. Farmers were further divided into five types: landlords, rich peasants, middle peasants, poor peasants, and hired laborers. Merchants were divided into rich merchants, middle merchants, stall vendors, and small merchants. Workers were also categorized based on their circumstances. For example, workers with knowledgeable or wealthy merchant/rich peasant brothers or relatives inevitably faced discrimination. The so-called middle merchants, middle peasants, and intellectuals were all classified as reactionaries and were often in danger of being killed. Near the fake Soviet government in Zhufushan, ninety-six pits were dug, and over 13,000 people were killed. In Mapu, the number of people killed was even higher, reaching over 30,000. The people's minds were even more frighteningly numbed. Even women and children would immediately say, "This is a landlord, that is a middle peasant, they do not comply with our party's discipline and should be eliminated," and so on.

Currently, within the disaster area, aside from the yellow-faced and emaciated survivors, there are only piles of white bones and skulls everywhere. After the bandits left, the people's harvest averaged only four dou of rice per person, and it is estimated that they can barely maintain their livelihood until the end of the year. However, next year's famine in the spring will require external grain relief, and seeds, plows, and agricultural tools have all been completely destroyed and should be provided. Secondly, changing people's thinking and breaking through the Communist Party's remaining organization are urgent tasks. After the group returns to the province, the party will present the situation in the disaster area to the provincial government and the central government, requesting prompt allocation of funds for emergency relief. On the one hand, they will appeal to fellow villagers abroad. Wuhu is the leading commercial area in Anhui province. We respectfully ask all sectors to have compassion, rise up together, and cooperate in providing relief. (7th)

The Lanzhou Water Tobacco Industry Declines Sharply

Stagnant Sales in Shanghai and Tianjin Markets Lead to Continued Closures of Gaolan Tobacco Farmers 73

Gaolan Dispatch: The Lanzhou water tobacco industry has gradually declined since the start of the Songhu War due to the loss of sales markets. Yesterday, this reporter met with a gentleman from the water tobacco industry to inquire about the recent situation. According to him, there were very few tobacco planters in Lanzhou this year, and the tobacco industry is even more depressed than in early spring. The reason is that the price of tobacco in Shanghai and Tianjin has plummeted. Last year, it was worth about one and a half taels of silver per catty, but now it has fallen to two fen or one tael, and there are still no buyers. Therefore, the water tobacco transported from Lanzhou to Tianjin and Shanghai last year is now all stockpiled. In previous years, Shanghai tobacco merchants would come to Lanzhou in early summer to order water tobacco, but this year, no one has inquired so far. As a result, very few tobacco farmers are planting, estimated to be less than 50-60% of the past. As for the so-called "Four Great Tobacco Firms" in Lanzhou, they have also suffered greatly due to excessive spending in recent years. Now, the large firms have closed down, and the number of small workshops that have stopped operating is even more uncountable. Therefore, the Lanzhou water tobacco industry is currently in a sharp decline. Although there were discussions about rectification around the beginning of this year, nothing has materialized. If it is delayed further, the Lanzhou tobacco industry will be beyond saving. (December 7th)

Songjiang 74

(Dragon King Temple Misleads Villagers) The Maota area, bordering Songjiang and Jinshan, is located on the shore of Maohu Lake, about thirty miles from Songjiang City. There is a Dragon King Temple there. In the past, Taibao Ashu looted the entire town of Zhangyan, and the kidnapped victims were brought to this temple to determine the price of their ransom, like a judicial trial. However, last year, rumors suddenly spread that there was an extraordinary monk in the temple, and superstitious people from far and wide hired boats to go there to worship and seek fortune, causing quite a stir. Even people from Suzhou and Wuxi came after hearing the news. The Jinshan County government then sent police to ban it, but the incense remained as strong as ever after the police left. Some boat merchants catered to the psychology of superstitious men and women, even opening special routes to transport them, making a great profit. The county government finally suppressed it severely, burning the wooden idols, and this trend gradually subsided. However, recently, the old habits have resurfaced. It is said that someone with a strange illness was cured by taking medicine from the temple, and this spread throughout the surrounding villages, causing ignorant people to burn incense and pray. The gathering is substantial. It is heard that the authorities will soon ban it to eliminate superstition.

Suzhou 75

(Yutai Steamer Robbed Midway) Suzhou long-distance telephone dispatch: Yesterday at about 3 PM, the Yutai small steamer of the China Merchants Bureau, sailing from Suzhou to Dongting East Mountain, was attacked when it reached Wangyang, Taihu Lake. Over twenty bandits jumped out of three bandit boats, boarded the steamer, and robbed it. Four passengers were kidnapped, and two passengers were shot dead on the spot. All valuables were looted. A patrol boat of the Eighth Water Police Team followed behind the steamer, providing protection. Upon hearing the alarm, they opened fire to apprehend the bandits, but unfortunately, the bandits outnumbered the police, injuring three policemen. All firearms were also robbed. It is now heard that the Third Water Police District has dispatched a large team to pursue and suppress the bandits.

I have repeatedly telegraphed to request exemption, but I was informed that due to the urgency of bandit suppression and the lack of funds for the military, this measure was unavoidable, limited to one year. Your consideration of the people's difficulties is greatly appreciated. However, when the second installment of land tax was collected this year, it was still ordered to be increased by two yuan, causing widespread panic and unspeakable hardship. This county has suffered continuous years of famine, and the people are living in poverty. This year, a general reduction of 80% has been approved, but even the regular quota of tax is still difficult to meet. How can there be any surplus to bear the increased grain tax? Xiaochu and others, entrusted by the local elders, dare not remain silent. Therefore, we urgently telegraph, humbly requesting that your department promptly order the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to exempt the increased winter grain tax from collection, to alleviate the people's suffering."

Changshu 81

He returned to Changshu on the evening of the 7th. When his self-provided Jing'an steamboat sailed to the vicinity of Qingdun Temple in Likou, it was already dark and he could not distinguish directions. At that time, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's regular liner, the Jiali, also sailed through the area. Due to the darkness, they could not see each other clearly, resulting in a collision between the two sides. Because the steamboat was weak, it was eventually broken and the entire boat was almost sunk. Fortunately, there was a ferry boat nearby that sailed close to the ship and ferried Captain Yang Qingjiu and others to the shore, saving them from disaster. After a while, the steamboat completely sank to the bottom of the river. Yang et al. then took the China Merchants Bureau's Jiali back to Suzhou. The next morning, he hired laborers in Suzhou and went to Qingdun Temple to salvage the steamboat. He found that most of the machinery was severely damaged. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is responsible for transporting it to Shanghai for repairs and compensation. Captain Yang returned to Changshu on the 8th and then transferred to Tiehengsha to suppress bandits.

Bai Wenwei and Zhang Zhiben Returned to Shanghai from Guangdong Yesterday Morning

The Content of the Proposal by the Central Committee Members in Guangdong Has Been Decided, and Four Central Committee Members Will Arrive in Shanghai on the 10th. Donations to Support the Volunteer Army are Very Enthusiastic. 89

Sun Ke, Li Liejun, and other Central Committee members in Shanghai, considering that the Third Plenary Session of the Fourth Central Committee has been scheduled to be held in Nanjing on the 15th of this month, have repeatedly consulted on the issues for the proposal. According to Bai Wenwei, the task of this trip south was not only to seek the opinions of the Central Committee members in Guangdong on the proposals for the Third Plenary Session, but also to discuss and plan methods for providing relief to the Northeast Volunteer Army and refugees. As for the proposals for the Third Plenary Session, the Central Committee members in Guangdong have decided that the content of the proposal will advocate active resistance against Japan externally and thorough suppression of bandits internally. Japan's advances have reached the point of unbearable tolerance. Although the indignation of the national populace is strong, there has been no concrete method of recovery for the lost Northeast. As for Liu Luyin, he will return to Shanghai a few days later because he still has unfinished business. Since the September 18th Incident, all parts of Guangdong Province have been actively boycotting Japanese goods. Therefore, Japanese goods have disappeared within Guangdong Province. The excellence of the results is incomparable to Shanghai. During my stay in Guangdong for several days, I only saw one Japanese woman along the way. This alone is enough to prove that Guangdong Province's anti-Japanese achievements are better than other places. Bai also said that Guangdong Province's monthly income is 11 million yuan, so the various local constructions are becoming more and more complete.

According to Zhang Zhiben, Guangdong Province's anti-Japanese enthusiasm is increasing day by day, so there are complete methods for assisting the Northeast Volunteer Army. It is hoped that the anti-Japanese resolution will be passed in the Third Plenary Session and efforts will be made to implement it. It has not yet been decided whether I will attend the Third Plenary Session.

The Central Government System Will Not Be Changed 90

Central News Agency: Chen Gongbo, the Minister of Industry, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing at about 8 AM yesterday. Chen talked in detail with the Central News Agency reporter about the Third Plenary Session and the steel plant and Construction Bank sponsored by the Ministry of Industry. They are described below.

Director Wang has no opinion on the National Participation Affairs, and it is feared that this case will not be submitted to the general meeting for discussion. Although there are various rumors about the merger of the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Communications, it has not been decided yet.

Therefore, the Ministry of Industry has formulated an entire fishery plan, advocating the establishment of more fishery associations and other institutions beneficial to fishermen to provide guidance and seek improvement. In short, the principle is to take from the fishery and use it for the fishery. As for the matter of my concurrently serving as the director of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fishery Bureau, it has not been decided yet.

(Steel Plant Contract Still Awaits Signature) The steel plant contract is still being investigated regarding the quality and quantity of the coal reserves in Leijiagou, and it will take some time before it is signed. As for the Construction Bank, it is actively proceeding. I have no important task in coming to Shanghai and must return to Nanjing within two or three days.
