The Municipal Government Will Refer the Jin Che Case to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs

Due to the Japanese Consul's Reply to the Protest, Not Acknowledging Jin as a Chinese National 95

The Shanghai Municipal Government previously protested to both the French and Japanese consulates regarding the Japanese consulate's dispatch of police to the French Concession to arrest Jin Che, a naturalized Korean. The Japanese side has now replied to the Municipal Government, stating that they recognize Jin as a Korean national. The Municipal Government will refer this matter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for handling. As Huang Zhanying may appear, the secret facts related to this case involving Ji Zhuqing will be temporarily withheld from publication. Details of the situation are recorded below.

(Content of the Reply) According to a statement from a person in charge of the Municipal Government, the Japanese side has sent a reply to the protest letter regarding the unauthorized arrest of Jin Che. The content of the reply indicates that they do not recognize Jin Che as a naturalized Chinese national. The reason they hold this view is that the Municipal Government considers Jin et al. to be Chinese citizens because they hold Naturalization Certificates No. 67 from the Ministry of Interior of the Chinese National Government. However, according to Japanese law, anyone who naturalizes in another country must first obtain permission from the Japanese government to renounce Japanese nationality before their acquired nationality is valid. An investigation reveals that Jin et al. did not obtain permission from the Japanese government, so their acquired Chinese nationality is invalid. The Japanese side still recognizes Jin et al. as Korean residents.

(Referral to the Ministry) A person in charge of the Municipal Government told the New Voice News Agency yesterday morning that the Japanese reply is not in accordance with international law. Since the Japanese side does not recognize Jin's Chinese nationality, Jin's international status becomes one of dual nationality. According to international law, in the event of a dispute involving a person with dual nationality, the nationality of the country where the person is located should be handled. Therefore, in this case, Jin Che is a person with dual nationality, and the Japanese side's unauthorized arrest is unreasonable. Therefore, the Municipal Government will refer this matter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for legal handling, as it falls under the purview of diplomatic affairs. As for the protest lodged with the French Consulate, the Japanese Consulate has returned the property after Jin Che was released, so the responsibility of the French side seems to be complete.

(Huang Zhanying's Letter) At 4:00 PM on the ninth day, in addition to receiving a letter from Wu Chengyu, Ji Zhuqing received another letter. Upon opening it, he realized it was from Huang Zhanying. He urgently asked where the messenger was, but they had already left. The original letter was very long, mainly stating that he was truly wronged and requested redress. At the end of the letter, he wrote, "The letter that your brother sent to Mr. Zhao was sent by registered mail. The return address is your brother's place. However, I did not obtain your consent beforehand. Please forgive your brother's presumption. Only you can save my life, and only you can redress my grievance. I hope you will redress it for me. I am extremely grateful and await your orders."

(Ji Zhuqing's Letter) After receiving the letter, Ji Zhuqing sent a special letter to various newspapers for publication, as follows: New Voice News Agency to all newspapers, please publish in the letter column: Brother Huang Zhanying, although we met through Wu Chengyu's introduction, our relationship is very good. If we do not clarify the situation at this critical juncture of life and death, it would be suicide for both the country and ourselves. This case has been going on for nine days. Why hasn't Mr. Huang come forward to surrender? Since you have been wronged, you should have explained it earlier. Why are you so foolish? If the evidence is solid, the people will have their own opinion, and I alone cannot do anything. If Mr. Huang unfortunately passes away at this time, wouldn't it be a wrongful death in the afterlife? If Mr. Huang is really sick and has no money for treatment, I will be responsible for the medical expenses. I hope you will come forward immediately, or let me know your location. I eagerly await your reply. Also, to the editors of various newspapers, regarding the Wu Chengyu and Huang Zhanying incident, before the truth is revealed, please publish both sides' statements equally to allow the public to make a fair judgment. I have been a friend of Wu Chengyu for many years and have no personal grudges. This negotiation is entirely for the public good. Who is right and who is wrong will be determined. If Mr. Wu is indeed innocent, I will apologize with a cane on my back. I will not break my word. I hereby inform you. Best wishes.

Indignation of Customs Officials Regarding Ernst's Actions

Calling for the Recovery of His Pension and Requesting the Government to Issue an Arrest Warrant 96

The Shanghai Evening Post and Mercury reported the previous day that Ernst (a Briton), the former Acting Inspector General of Customs, is now employed as a customs advisor to the puppet Manchurian regime and will be appointed as the Inspector General of Customs for the puppet state. Records of the Inspection of the Completed Dike Construction by the National Government Flood Relief Committee (12) 99

(Lunch at Wuhan University) The inspection team was originally scheduled to go to Qingshan, Wuchang, on the morning of the fourth to inspect the Wuhui Dike. Due to rain and strong winds, the ferry was inconvenient, so the trip was temporarily canceled. The Provincial Government had five cars ready at the Hanyang Wharf, and they took them to Luojia Mountain, arriving in about 40 minutes. Luojia Mountain is located in the eastern suburbs of Wuchang and has excellent scenery. The new campus of Wuhan University is built on the mountainside in a palace-style architecture. From a distance, the green tiles and yellow walls surrounding the green mountains are exceptionally beautiful. After entering, they were guided by the Provincial Government and Xiong Guozhao, the director of Wuhan University's affairs, to the meeting room to rest. From the window, you could see East Lake, the lake water was green, and the trees were lush, as if you were in a painting. Then, they visited the library, science museum, auditorium, dining room, and other places. In front of the school is a very large square with complete sports facilities. At that time, the Provincial Government had prepared a simple meal in the Wuhan University cafeteria, and they took their seats for lunch. At about 2:00 PM, each team member left the school, crossed the river, and returned to Hankou.

(Tea Party at the Commander-in-Chief's Office) At 4:00 PM on the fourth, Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission and Commander-in-Chief of the Anti-Banditry Campaign in Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Provinces, held a tea party on the second floor of the Jin Cheng Bank to entertain the Dike Construction Inspection Team and the visiting delegations from Nanjing and Beiping to the recovered bandit areas. Chiang, wearing a Chinese-style jacket and cotton robe, was full of energy and delivered a welcoming speech, stating briefly that he was very pleased to gather with the Chinese and foreign members of the Dike Construction Inspection Team and the Bandit Area Inspection Team during this time of national crisis and bandit suppression. He hoped that everyone would offer their guidance and opinions, and he would accept them sincerely. He had prepared refreshments to express his welcome and gratitude to those who had traveled a long way to inspect.

Surplus Jiangxi Rice Is Transported to Guangdong for Sale

The Only Good Way to Relieve Jiangxi Farmers 100

The farmland in the provinces along the Yangtze River has had a bumper harvest this year. Hunan, Jiangxi, and Anhui have mostly had ten-year-old yields. The price of Xiang and Gan rice has fallen to 2.5 to 2.6 yuan per stone. Hunan initially planned to relax the ban on 2 million stone, but the heavy donations and taxes exceeded the value of the rice, resulting in purchasers being insufficient. The same is true in Jiangxi. Now, Jiangxi farmers have too much rice stockpiled and cannot sell it for a while. Even if they sell it at a lower price, few people ask about it, resulting in a situation where grain is cheap and farmers are harmed, and the countryside goes bankrupt.

(The Provincial Government Seeks Relief) The Jiangxi Provincial Government, in view of the excessive stockpiles of grain,

and the abundant harvests in many places, and because Shanghai rice merchants have stopped purchasing due to the import of foreign rice and wheat, is seeking other ways to save the situation. Since the coastal provinces in South China have a huge demand for rice each year, millions of stone of Anhui rice have been gathered in Guangdong Province. Jiangxi Province has also decided to follow suit. The Provincial Government will initiate and organize a large-scale transportation and sales cooperative to connect leaders from all walks of life in the province to handle Jiangxi rice exports, tentatively set at 1 million stone, to be sold to Guangdong first. With the consent of Chairman Xiong Shihui, personnel have been sent to Guangdong to contact grain merchants and reach an agreement. At the same time, donations and taxes will be reduced to quickly sell out the province's stockpiled rice, thereby relieving the farmers. The cooperative has been established and has begun to rent ships to transport rice.

(Telegraph Rental of Ocean Liners to Transport to Guangdong) With the Provincial Government leading the export of Jiangxi rice, it is easy to achieve success. Chairman Xiong telegraphed Shanghai to contact Yu Qiaqing of the Sanbei Company to rent ships. The telegram stated: Jiangxi has too much rice stockpiled, and the countryside is in decline. The Provincial Government has now contacted all sectors to organize a large-scale transportation and sales cooperative to relieve the farmers in the province and sell the surplus grain. We plan to transport rice to Guangdong. Everything has been negotiated. We intend to rent ocean liners from your company to load and transport the rice. Please provide a special low price for the ship and water feet and telegraph us immediately so that we can rent the ships and go to Jiujiang to load and transport to Guangdong. Yu has agreed to rent the ships at a low price to facilitate the people's food supply and has telegraphed Chairman Xiong to prepare to release the ships for loading and transportation.

Page 11

(Xu Shiying's Reply) Xu Shiying was then publicly recommended by the Dike Construction Inspection Team to deliver a thank-you speech. He briefly stated, "Commander-in-Chief, military commanders, administrative officials, guests, and colleagues, we are here in Hankou to participate in the dike construction inspection and are deeply grateful for the Commander-in-Chief's grand reception and encouragement. Last year's floods caused the dikes in the Jiang, Huai, and Han rivers to be almost completely destroyed. The losses suffered by the three towns of Wuhan were particularly severe. Everyone present knows this. After the floods, the government immediately sent people to handle relief, epidemic prevention, and sanitation work. At the same time, the National Government Flood Relief Committee was specially organized, with Director Song serving as the chairman, and various departments were set up to handle relief work. The personnel in charge of dike construction have always been exceptionally diligent. Now, all the dike projects in the Jiang, Huai, and Han rivers have been completed. Although we only saw a part of the dike construction during this inspection along the river, the general consensus is that the dike construction is extremely solid. There has been a lot of rain this summer, but the highest water level is still one or two meters away from the dike surface. The fields along the river have been well protected, and as a result, none of them have been flooded. This autumn, the harvest is very abundant, and the people are grateful for the government's grace. As a member of the inspection team, I believe that the dike construction was able to achieve such a great and remarkable project in the shortest time with the most economical plan, which is truly admirable. After passing through the four provinces of Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei, the economy of the rural areas along the river has indeed recovered a lot compared to last year. The internal banditry has been largely stabilized after several months of suppression by the Bandit Suppression Headquarters. Regarding this point, we especially admire the Commander-in-Chief's virtue and his spirit of perseverance and the efforts of the military and political leaders present. Since we want to comfort our compatriots in these recovered disaster areas, after receiving the Commander-in-Chief's telegram on the 30th, people from all walks of life in Shanghai, such as Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Du Pengsheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Ye Juhu, Zheng Shaojue, Chen Aishi, Wang Rutang, Wu Zhihao, Qu Wenliu, Huang Hanzhi, and Zhao Jinqing, Wu Tiecheng, the Mayor of Shanghai, and Mr. Wen Lantin, Li Zushen, and Sun Chunqi, immediately organized a Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Charity Association to raise relief funds. They are all very enthusiastic, so we have made considerable preparations in terms of relief funds. Before we departed from Shanghai, the association invited many leaders to come to Hankou to express our gratitude to the Commander-in-Chief before visiting various places. The representatives elected by various groups could not come due to time constraints, but they may come later. When we return to Shanghai, we will certainly make extra efforts to raise funds for those disaster victims. This is our bounden duty, and only in this way can we live up to the efforts of the Commander-in-Chief and the military and political leaders present. We should each fulfill our responsibilities. Today, we are grateful for the Commander-in-Chief's reception. On behalf of everyone who has come, I express our sincere gratitude and wish the Commander-in-Chief and his wife good health. Xu Shiying finished his speech.

Cao Fengchun, Representative of the Righteous Army in Western Liaoning, Writes to Request Assistance

Righteous Soldiers Still Wear Single Layers in the Freezing Cold 103

Mr. Cao Fengchun, the Shanghai representative of Geng Jizhou, Commander-in-Chief of the Righteous Army in Western Liaoning, wrote to the Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe Righteous Army Support Association yesterday to request relief. The original letter stated: Sir, unfortunately, on the night of September 18 last year, Japanese imperialism suddenly attacked the three northeastern provinces. The border defense officers were unprepared in advance and adhered to a policy of non-resistance afterward. The people of Northeast China, unwilling to see their country broken apart, would rather die resisting than be cowardly subjects of a subjugated nation. They successively organized righteous armies and fought to the death with the Japanese invaders. Our army has fought for a year in hundreds of battles, large and small. Although we cannot drive the enemy out of the country, we can make the Japanese bandits exhausted. However, the reason why we cannot recover lost territory is not because our soldiers are not brave, but because of the lack of food and ammunition. Sincerely, I came south to request that all sectors give our army practical assistance to kill the enemy. Since arriving in Shanghai, it has been more than two months. Although I have tried my best to run around and have shouted myself hoarse, the only assistance I have received is 347 sets of cotton clothing from the Righteous Army Support Association. It is a drop in the bucket. The suffering on the front lines is truly indescribable. At this time, it is already freezing cold outside, and the righteous soldiers who are fighting bloody battles are still wearing single layers. Now, I am glad to hear that the gentlemen of your association are deeply concerned about the situation in the Northeast. It is likely that the suffering of our fighting righteous soldiers can be slightly relieved. I have learned that Fudan University has donated more than 1,000 sets of cotton clothing to your association. I am writing to you specifically to ask that your association immediately give it to our army. I will immediately transport it to the front lines to strengthen our army. I also request assistance. I urgently submit my request and await your reply.

Recent Reports on the Establishment of a Bill Clearing House by the Banking Sector

Can Save Exchange Procedures, Location in the Banking Association 109

The banking sector in this city, feeling the troublesome and laborious back-and-forth procedures of bill exchange, has referred to the practices of various European and Western countries to organize a bill clearing house. The clearing house has decided to be established in January next year. The various news about the clearing house is recorded below.

Motivation for Organization 110

According to Mr. Lin Kanghou, Secretary-General of the Banking Association, bill clearing houses have long been established in various Western countries. The banking industry in our country is not yet fully developed, so it is still lacking. In fact, this is an indispensable organization. Because there are quite a few banks in Shanghai, each bank issues checks, drafts, etc., and each bank receives many banknotes from other banks every day. If these banknotes are instructed to be exchanged at each bank, then the back-and-forth movement will be overwhelmed. Therefore, a bill clearing house is organized, and each bank sends personnel to the office to exchange and offset the immediate bills received, saving the journey and time. Its convenience need not be repeated.

Location Issues 111

The clearing house is jointly organized by the Bank Association's United Reserve Division. Before the bank's construction of the clubhouse, the affiliated sites, such as the bank club and the foundation committee, were within the plan. The location of the bill clearing house was also in the plan. The association has surplus housing, so the location is also in the bank club.

To Be Established Next Month 112

As for the establishment date, it could have been done sooner. However, due to the current year-end season and the heavy workload of account settlement and liquidation for various banks, it has to be slightly delayed. It is expected to be established around January of next year (i.e., next month). Because the organizational procedures are simple, the banks that have currently joined the association include China Bank, Bank of Communications, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, China Industrial Bank, China Reclamation Bank, Commercial Bank, Central China Bank, China National Encouragement Bank, and dozens of others.

Municipal Police Bureau Re-investigates Household Registration 113

The household registration investigation in this city has recently been re-investigated by various district offices in sections. They are paying particular attention to the increase or decrease of households, as well as the entry and exit of maids and servants. With the year-end approaching, this is to prevent petty thieves from taking the opportunity to steal. However, many residents often neglect to report the employment of maids in their homes, resulting in fines of five or ten yuan being discovered by various districts. This has been frequently heard lately, and it is hoped that residents in the South City will pay attention to it.

Yesterday's Trial of Zhu Tieying Case

Newspaper Publication Is Based on Submitted Articles, Newspaper Is the Voice of the Public 122

Zhu Tieying, the editor of the Taicang Moye Daily, was sued by Hu Jiacong, the director of the business tax bureau, to the Taicang County Government for publishing satirical articles about the illegal collection of business tax. Zhu refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the Shanghai District Court. Yesterday, the criminal court judge Qian Chengjun, along with judges Shen Youqi and Guan Liting, held a continued hearing. According to the official report submitted by Hu Jiacong, the provincial government issued an order to urge the collection of taxes before August 19, and received the exemption order on the 26th. According to the tax collection investigator, Zhu Jungang, he received a small amount in Shuangfeng Town on September 17, but later failed to collect any more. Therefore, he and four others made an official report. This report was done by phone, so they reported the facts. Qian Tiemin testified that the merchants in Shuangfeng refused to pay because of the newspaper report that they were stealing chickens, and they could not collect taxes elsewhere. Therefore, they delayed the report until the 26th, and on the afternoon of the 26th, they received the exemption order from the bureau while they were outside. Zhu Tieying testified that the publication was based on submitted articles, and the provincial government gazette of August 10 stated that the 518th meeting decided to exempt the counties of Tai, Jia, and Bao separately. As for why it was not corrected, it was corrected on the 23rd, and the provincial government also announced the method, so there was no need to correct it, and presented two copies of the gazette as evidence. At this point, the official requested the prosecutor Yang Qi to present his opinion, and then the defendant's lawyer defended, mainly arguing that the newspaper's mission is to be the voice of the public and has the responsibility to supervise the government. Now that the exemption order has been issued, there is no crime of harming the country. The government is composed of the people, and the interests of the people are the interests of the country. Please declare innocence. The official announced the end of the debate, and the verdict will be announced on the 15th.

Although they set up their stalls on the roadside, they do not obstruct traffic or pose a hygiene hazard. There is no real need to ban them. Their situation is truly pitiable. Therefore, we jointly sign and stamp this petition, requesting Your Excellency the Director-General to extend your benevolence to those under your jurisdiction and to understand the hardships of the common people. We ask that you allow them to return to their original state and continue to set up their stalls as usual. With the severe cold approaching, this would save the stallholders from the suffering of cold and hunger. They will all sing praises of Your Excellency's boundless virtue. Two Bureaus Issue Public Notice on Measures to Ban the Buying and Selling of Used Copper Wire 133

Public Notice from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities and the Public Security Bureau: Regarding the issuance of a joint public notice. Considering that telephones are of utmost importance to transportation and public safety, especially during the winter prevention period, they must be strictly protected. Recently, there have been frequent incidents of telephone line theft. Although various district offices have solved cases and brought culprits to justice, ignorant and stubborn people, greedy for petty gains, are willing to risk the law, and the theft trend has not diminished. Unless the outlet for stolen goods is cut off, it will be insufficient to deter the wicked. The Shanghai Telephone Bureau has drafted five measures to ban the buying and selling of used copper wire, which have been jointly submitted by this bureau and others to the municipal government for approval. In addition to the Public Security Bureau sending a letter to the police departments of the two concessions to assist in implementation, this notice is hereby issued for public knowledge and compliance. If anyone dares to engage in private buying and selling, they will be severely punished without leniency upon detection. Let each be warned. Attached is a copy of the measures to ban the buying and selling of used copper wire: (1) All copper, tin, and five-metal smelting factories, electrical supply stores, and various scrap dealerships are prohibited from buying or selling all kinds of used copper, iron wire, and cables. However, this does not apply to the purchase or sale of old electrical wires from official communication agencies with a certificate of proof. (2) Smelting factories that purchase used copper wire or lead-sheathed cables must apply to the local Public Security Bureau in advance for inspection and obtain a permit. If the Public Security Bureau has doubts about the source of the wire, it may seal it first and notify the telecommunications agency for joint investigation. (3) Anyone transporting used copper wire or cables out of the country must have the carrier verify the certificate before allowing shipment. If the carrier does not have the certificate, they should immediately notify the Public Security Bureau to detain and investigate. (4) The Public Security Bureau has the right to inspect such factories and shops at any time. The telecommunications agency may also notify the Public Security Bureau to send personnel to conduct joint inspections when necessary. Anyone carrying various kinds of old electrical wires in public places without the certificate specified in Article 1 may be detained and investigated by the Public Security Bureau at any time. (5) Violators of Articles 1 to 3 may be prosecuted by the Public Security Bureau according to law for receiving stolen goods. Issued on December of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Huang Boqiao, Director of the Bureau of Public Utilities; Wen Hong'en, Director of the Public Security Bureau.

Songhu and Yangtze River Pilots' Grand Alliance

Hai Bu Gives... Organizing a Guild 137

Piloting, also known as guiding, is essential for ships entering and leaving ports and rivers, ensuring the safety of navigation. Major powers have extremely strict regulations, and some even have special provisions prohibiting non-citizens from serving as pilots. In our country, the piloting business is mostly controlled by foreigners, which is the most serious case of selling out rights. The Yangtze River is our country's inland river, and allowing foreign ships to navigate it is a special agreement. As for private piloting, there are no such provisions. Currently, there are 24 Europeans and Americans and 21 Japanese privately acting as pilots outside the Cheng Hankuan customs. During the January 28th Incident, Japanese warships were able to enter our territory and destroy our Song Fortress and raid our capital, all due to these foreign pilots. If we did not have foreign pilots to guide them, they would not know our waterways, even with strong ships and sharp armor, because they are unfamiliar with our currents and sandbanks. Furthermore, foreign merchant ships entering our inland rivers are monopolized by foreign pilots, reversing the roles of host and guest, and the piloting business is increasingly shrinking. Chinese pilots are facing an even steeper decline. Yang Hanlin and others at the Preparatory Office of the Songhu Pilots' Guild in this city, in order to rescue the piloting business and safeguard navigation rights, have proposed a grand alliance of pilots to resist the encroachment of foreign pilots and plan to further petition the government to ban foreign pilots on the Yangtze River. A summary of the situation is reported as follows:

Reasons for the Alliance: The Yangtze River pilots in this city are divided into three groups: Zou, Zhejiang, and Guangdong, forming four guilds with a total of about 300 members. In addition to two-thirds of the pilots who are long-term employees of the six major shipping companies in this city for their Yangtze River routes, about 100 pilots are hired on a temporary basis. They lack unity and each acts for their own benefit. Whenever a ship sails on the Yangtze River, they compete for piloting jobs and drastically lower fees, disrupting the business and damaging the industry. Furthermore, there are those who lack experience and fill positions with unqualified individuals, risking valuable ships. In order to maintain the shipping industry and regulate the trade, it has been decided to form an alliance for cooperation.

▲Unity Measures: Yang and others from the Preparatory Office proposed that all pilots should unite and operate openly, avoiding the drastic competition of uneven fees. Yang convened all pilots to explain this purpose, and everyone expressed their agreement. The unity measures mainly involve uniting all pilots, organizing a guild, and providing services according to the qualifications of each pilot. Then, the general piloting office will distribute assignments fairly to ensure uniform fees and prevent unauthorized increases or decreases, thereby maintaining the livelihoods of the pilots.

Guaranteeing Navigation: After the pilots' grand alliance is formed and the guild is established, internal strife among colleagues can be eliminated, and piloting fees will be unified. Once the qualifications of the pilots have been assessed, shipping companies can avoid the various concerns of hiring temporary pilots. The safety of ships depends on the competence of the pilots. In the future, shipping companies only need to notify the guild when hiring pilots, and the guild will carefully select qualified pilots. This measure is also significant for guaranteeing navigation. It is reported that the various shipping companies and marine insurance associations in this city have expressed their support.

Business Licenses: The guild recently received instructions from the Naval Pilot Training Institute, stating that the institute had previously trained and issued certificates of completion to Yangtze River pilots, and now, based on the assessment of their qualifications, the institute should stamp the certificates to allow them to conduct business. The guild has notified all pilots to register with the guild before December 31 this year in order to apply for business licenses.

Piloting Fee Issue: It has been decided that the piloting fees will be implemented uniformly from January 1 next year, without any increase. Furthermore, special conveniences will be provided for foreign merchant ships and warships. The guild is located at No. 36 Sijing Road in this city.

Hong immediately reported to the front desk, who in turn reported to the Laozha Police Station. Detective Cao Qishan was ordered to investigate and sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but he died shortly after. The body was taken to the Philomene Road morgue. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court was requested to send Prosecutor Zhang Yaoguang to the morgue to examine the body. Upon taking his seat in court, Detective Cao Qishan stated in his report that when he went to the hotel to investigate, the deceased was unable to speak and there were no suicide notes or opium. Therefore, he was sent to the hospital for treatment. Tea boy Hong Ahe also testified about the situation at the time. Zhang then ruled that the deceased, Pan Mi, a male, had indeed died of poisoning. The body was handed over to Huang Bingchen, who signed a guarantee to collect the body for burial.

Private Theft of Eighty Boxes of Raisins

Worth 494 Taels of Silver 140

Lou Yuanxing, a clerk at the American raisin company located at No. 3 Guangdong Road, took eighty boxes of raisins worth 494 taels of silver from the Dis Wei Road warehouse at 4:30 PM on the 8th of this month. He hired a cart to transport them to the Huaxing Canned Food Company at No. 706 North Sichuan Road for temporary storage. Lou then hid at the home of Yi in Dayuan Lane No. 380, Adyat Road, planning to sell the raisins. The company discovered the theft the day before and reported it to the Dis Wei Road police station. Chinese and Western detectives were dispatched to arrest Lou and retrieve the stolen goods from the Huaxing Company. Yesterday morning, they were handed over to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The police station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated that the case originated because the company had recently placed orders with the Wansheng Canned Food Company in the Chinese-controlled Nanshi area and the Huaxing Company on North Sichuan Road. Wansheng ordered 80 boxes and Huaxing ordered 15 boxes. The defendant then used a 100-tael check from the China & South Bank on North Sichuan Road, along with 40 yuan in cash, to take delivery of the goods in the name of Wansheng. It was found that the check was issued by Huaxing. The lawyer requested that the defendant be detained temporarily because the witnesses were not present in court today. He requested that the court summon the owner of Wansheng Company in Nanshi and the bank staff to testify about who the check was issued to and how much Wansheng Company ordered. Huaxing Company stated that the order was only for 15 boxes, and the defendant transported a large quantity of raisins, claiming that the rest were temporarily stored. There were some doubts. After Judge Zhao Linyu briefly questioned the defendant, he was returned to custody, and the case was adjourned to summon witnesses for further verification.

Robbery on Beijing Road, Zhabei 142

Fang Jinji Shop, located at No. 374 Beijing Road, Zhabei, specializes in melting metal items. At 7:40 PM last night, the shop's employees were preparing to close for the day when three robbers suddenly appeared outside the door. One was wearing a black overcoat, one was wearing a blue cloth long gown, and one was wearing a gray cloth long gown. Two of the robbers were carrying pistols. Upon entering, they used their guns to threaten the employees into silence. The employees were terrified and dared not move, allowing the robbers to search and loot the premises. As a result, they stole two taels and seven maces of pure gold, three taels of silver, a pair of gold earrings, and 23 yuan in cash, worth a total of over 400 yuan. Gao Changsheng and Lu Ronggao Found Not Guilty in Car Theft Case 143

The Jiujiang Auto Shop on Jiujiang Road is owned by Lu Ronggao (also known as Lao San or A San), a native of Jiangbei. At 6:30 PM on the afternoon of the 24th of last month, automobile number 17531, parked on Yinghua Street, suddenly disappeared. The chauffeur, Li Asi, reported the theft to the police station and requested that they investigate. At 8:50 PM, the vehicle was found on Longmen Road. Constable No. 531 arrested the driver, Gao Changsheng from Zhenjiang, and took him and the car to the police station. Gao confessed that he had been ordered by Lu Ronggao, the owner of the Jiujiang Shop, to drive the car to Longmen Road to transport opium. Lu was then arrested and handed over to the First Special Court for questioning and detention. Details of the case were reported in this newspaper on the 3rd of this month. Yesterday morning, Presiding Judge Qian Hongye of the Special Court continued the hearing. The police station's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, stated that Lu Ronggao had previously claimed that he went to Hangzhou on the morning of the 22nd of last month. He presented Western Deputy Constable Howell as a witness to prove that he had met with Lu on the afternoon of the 22nd to prove that Lu's testimony was false. Howell testified that he had visited Lu at the Jiujiang Shop at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 22nd to discuss car matters. Lu's lawyer, Wu Linkun, stated that after Lu went to Hangzhou, he stayed at the home of Lu Baoshan in Tianzhu and invited him to come to Shanghai to testify, but he declined because he was not involved. The court then ordered the start of arguments. The lawyers for Gao Changsheng, Fan Gang and Wu Linkun, and the police station's lawyer, Ru, debated each other. The court ruled that the crime could not be proven and acquitted Gao and Lu. Ru requested that they be kept under bond pending an appeal, and the court granted the request.

Reader's Advisor

Discussion on Ms. Zhang Yunqiu's Proposed Question 145

Mr. Yu Yikong's Message: ⑴ Due to men's narrow-mindedness, ⑵ due to women's desire for commerce and vanity, ⑶ due to the inability of both parties to respect each other. ⑴ Remedial measures: ⑴ Mutual trust, ⑵ mutual hard work and self-encouragement, ⑶ mutual respect, love without obstruction.

Mr. Shen Qilu's Message: There are couples who live a lifetime without arguing. Let them argue. Remediation is not very effective.

Mr. Wei Qixiang's Message: ⑴ Due to the psychology of being unfaithful and liking the new and disliking the old, ⑵ the remedy is for both parties to reflect and reminisce, reflect on their own faults, and reminisce about past love, so that new love can arise from repentance.

Mr. Ying Zhifan's Message: ⑴ Due to the inability to control lust ⑵ one must work hard and remove desires.

Mr. Feng Juefei's Message: ⑴ Due to the actual inequality of the status of men and women, women can be owned by men, then men can fully exert their possessiveness according to their likes and dislikes, and thus tragedy is staged. ⑵ ⑴ The root cause must be to transform the social system, ⑵ the man must respect the woman's personality, ⑶ the woman must broaden her horizons and not be troubled by trivial family matters.

Mr. Zhang Chunbo's Message: ⑵ Because before marriage, both parties failed to carefully examine each other's temperament, but blindly pursued the opposite sex, and because of the oppression of life after marriage, ⑵ from the beginning, don't regard love as too mysterious, don't rely entirely on emotional impulses, you must use reason to think about everything, thoroughly understand each other's personality, determine the standard for the progress of love based on your own environment, and the woman must also seek independence in life and not always rely on her husband.

Mr. Ting Kui's Message: ⑴ Before marriage, both parties hide their weaknesses. After marriage, all weaknesses are exposed. ⑵ Before marriage, you must thoroughly understand each other. After marriage, if there is any disagreement, you must try your best to tolerate it. If it is impossible to tolerate, it is better to simply divorce.

Mr. Yu Yan's Message: ⑴ Due to usual frivolousness and mutual contempt, ⑵ when love is strong, you must not forget the word "etiquette". You should learn from Liang Hong and Meng Guang's mutual respect and courtesy.

Mr. Zhang Feiran's Message: ⑴ ⑴ Economic oppression, ⑵ women's inability to live independently, ⑶ the inability of the two sexes to reconcile spiritually. ⑵ ⑴ The fundamental way is to transform the social system, ⑵ it is necessary to enable women to obtain occupations and leave the family to become "people" of society.

Reporter's Note: Since this column submitted Ms. Zhang's question to the public for discussion on December 3, the letters received every day with suggestions have been extremely enthusiastic. Now, the accumulated letters have reached hundreds. It can be seen that the question raised by Ms. Zhang is also a question that most people are thinking about anxiously. In addition to the summaries of the letters that have been published in succession, after reviewing the remaining letters, there are no special insights. Publishing them one by one would only waste space. Therefore, it is decided that from today onwards, the discussion on this issue will be stopped. All opinions from all parties will be collected tomorrow and a conclusion will be made. Readers are requested to pay attention.

Mr. Qiu Qisou of Wumen: As stated in your letter, then you are an old friend of this newspaper. Please provide your mailing address so that we can communicate with you.

To all those who submit letters to this column: Please pay attention to the brief rules of this column in the future, otherwise we will not reply. The communication rules are reprinted below.

1. Scope of Issues

⑴ Politics and Economics ⑵ Law ⑶ Occupation ⑷ Marriage ⑸ Family ⑹ Education ⑺ Rural Areas ⑻ Natural Sciences ⑼ Medicine ⑽ Social Issues

2. Method of Correspondence

⑴ Write clearly your name, gender, age, occupation, (or school year and grade, native place, mailing address (detailed writing is still required when continuing communication.)

⑵ Secondly, raise the question you want to discuss. The text should be detailed, accurate, and easy for people to understand the true meaning.

3. Please write "Shenbao Reader Advisory Department Receipt" on the outside of the envelope and attach a considerable amount of return postage.

4. The imprint of the special issue of the Reader Advisory Column of this newspaper must be cut off and pasted on the upper left corner of the letter. Letters without the imprint will not be answered.

5. How to handle received letters

⑴ Respect the wishes of readers. All letters stating that they wish not to be answered in the newspaper, or that they do not wish to disclose their names when answering, can be handled accordingly.

⑵ If the letter does not state how to answer, but this newspaper believes that answering one person has reference value for the public, it will be disclosed in the newspaper.

⑶ If the letter states that it hopes to be answered in the newspaper, but is limited by space, only the main points can be disclosed; if it cannot be disclosed at all; or if the question requires detailed research, and the answer and disclosure have to be delayed, readers are requested to forgive us. However, those who cannot be answered in the newspaper will still be answered by letter.

Dongmen Road Fire

Zhu Chengzan Burned to Death 146

Yi Xing Foreign Goods Store, No. 24 Dongmen Road, outside Xiaodongmen, Nanshi, is divided into five departments: porcelain department, shoe department, galoshes department, sweater department, and sock department, all of which are jointly owned. The galoshes and sweater departments are managed by director Ge Baohua. The director of the porcelain department is named Mu Changchun, and the director of the shoe department is Yin. Usually, the income and expenses of each department are managed by the directors of each department, which is no different from setting up a stall. However, because the location of the store is suitable, the business is not bad. The total sales of various goods reach three to four hundred yuan per day. It has been open for more than half a year. Unexpectedly, at 0:30 yesterday morning, the store was not careful about fire and suddenly reported negligence. At that time, all the employees in the store had already gone to sleep. Fortunately, Li De, the seventh sentry policeman, noticed it and immediately broke open the gate of the store. The fire became more and more rampant, and flames pierced through the roof. After the Fire Brigade Association heard about it, it immediately rang the bell to report the news. The pump trucks from the fire brigades in each district rushed to the scene to connect the water and extinguish the fire. The employees in the store woke up from their dreams and fled out of their houses. Those who were staying upstairs saw that the stairs had been burned down and jumped out of the windows upstairs to escape. However, one of the employees named Zhu Chengzan, 21 years old, from Anhui, usually read novels and newspapers under the light after the store closed at about 9 pm, and did not sleep until about 11 pm, so he had to be called by others every morning to get up. When the fire broke out yesterday morning, although he was called by his colleagues, Zhu was sleeping soundly and did not wake up. He was forced to realize that the fire had started, and the room was filled with thick smoke. He fainted in an instant and could not escape, so he died in the fire. Before long, the fire was extinguished. The entire two-story building of the store was burned down. Zhu's body was found at the same time, his head and face were burnt, and it was unbearable to look at. Then the police took Xuan Wenchao, a shareholder of the store, to the first district. Under the preliminary trial by the district chief, because the store had fire insurance of 3,000 taels and the cause of the fire was unknown, in addition to sending the police to thoroughly investigate the truth of the fire, he prepared a document to send Xuan to the bureau for questioning. At the same time, he ordered the local chief to report to the local court to request an autopsy. At about 3 pm, Yang, the prosecutor entrusted by the court, and the coroner arrived at the scene and found that the deceased Zhu Chengzan was indeed burned to death by the fire. The body was handed over to his family to be coffined and buried, and a certificate was obtained for future reference. The coroner returned to the court after the autopsy.

The posthumous works of Mr. Mo Jiashi of Huating in the Former Ming Dynasty are published 147

Mr. Jiashi, the seventh ancestor of Mr. Mo Zijing, a local elder of Shanghai, whose name was Chengqing, courtesy name Zixian, and posthumous title Zhenbai, was a contemporary figure of Chen Xia and other gentlemen of the Jisha Society in the late Ming Dynasty. His extant works include the "Bangqiu An Anthology" and the "Caiyin Cao Poetry Collection." The Mo family was originally from Huating, and had been officials for generations. His great-grandfather, Duke Zhongjiang, named Ruzhong, and his grandfather, Duke Tinghan, named Shilong, wrote poetry and prose that illuminated the four directions. Because of the chaos of the world, the gentleman lived in seclusion in the western suburbs of Shanghai. When the dynasty changed, he immediately decided to burn books and enter the mountains. Whenever he felt indignant, he recorded poetry and prose to express his aspirations, such as the "Praise of the Marquis of Wu and Jingjie" and the "Biography of the Four Loyalists" in the collection. His writing is unrestrained and ancient, and the tailoring does not exceed a single word, and the meaning is self-contained beyond words. His poems are pure, profound, and free from all vulgarity. His engravings are so extreme that he disdains to mention a single word from his predecessors. This collection contains 40 prefaces, 25 biographies, 3 epitaphs, 7 tombstones, 9 sacrificial texts, 7 introductions, 10 books, 2 records, 2 essays, 3 explanations, 3 debates, 1 saying, 1 explanation, 13 praises, 6 inscriptions, 5 inscriptions, 8 postscripts, 2 epilogues, 2 chronicles, 11 ancient poems in four characters, 67 in five characters, 44 in seven characters, 37 quatrains in five characters, 5 in six characters, 97 in seven characters, 25 ranked poems in five characters, 275 regulated verses in five characters, 102 in seven characters, and 40 lyrics. The original manuscript is written in fine calligraphy, which is the gentleman's hand-copied version in his later years, and is a true treasure. Among them, many taboo words against the Manchu Qing Dynasty are found in the "Biographies of Loyalty and Righteousness" and the "Shanghai Chaos." Therefore, his grandson kept the manuscript hidden and did not show it to others easily. After the founding of the Republic of China, it was made public, and many errors were caused by repeated copying. Therefore, it was handed over to the Zhonghua Book Company to be printed and bound into a book in Song imitation type on high-quality paper, totaling four large volumes. The printing cost was relatively high, and not many books were published. Saoye Bookstore on Qipan Street, Songjiang Saoye Bookstore, and Yizhi Bookstore in this port all have them for sale, priced at two yuan, to spread them widely. Contemporary writers should have a copy on hand to read first.

The Jiande Society Cantonese Music Troupe is Disbanded 148

The Cantonese Music Troupe of the Zhonghua Jiande Society on Old Baizi Road and Fusheng Road in this port has been established for many years and has always served the society as its purpose. It has performed outside many times and has long enjoyed a good reputation. Recently, the troupe, in view of the fact that after the Shanghai War, the members were scattered and it was not easy to gather them, and that the director of the troupe, Mr. Huang Shaohua, also resigned due to his busy schedule and was unable to be retained, which resulted in no one in charge. Therefore, the troupe had to temporarily disband. All the professors and cadres introduced by the director resigned on the 10th of this month. Once talents are found, they will be restored.

Correspondence 157

Dear Sir, After investigating, this bureau was ordered to increase the quota of stamp tax. The method determined is to increase the original quota of each branch bureau by 20% uniformly. The increase is in the quota, not the tax rate. At the stamp tax meeting, it was clearly stated that the branch bureau chiefs should rectify and encourage sales and find ways to increase revenue in order to meet the quota, and should not be harsh due to the increase in quota. Now, I read in the newspaper that the local news column on the 9th of this month stated that the method of dispatch is that each branch bureau should uniformly increase 20% when collecting taxes. This is completely inconsistent with the facts. Fearing that a misunderstanding may arise, I am writing to you for correction in the Letter to the Editor column. Sincerely, Jiangsu Stamp Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau, Ministry of Finance, December 9.

Dear Sir, I was surprised to read a news item entitled "Detailed News of Rent Reduction and Exemption in North Sichuan Road" in the local news column of your newspaper on the 9th. After investigating, Sanxinli is managed by the law office of Dietback, and Yongfengfang and Xinxiangli are managed by the Wuhe Foreign Firm. There is no rent exemption for six months for Sanxinli and rent reduction of 30%, nor rent exemption for eight months and rent reduction of 40% for Yongfengfang and Xinxiangli as reported in your newspaper. We are sincerely concerned that inaccurate rumors may cause misunderstandings, so we are writing to you for correction and request that it be published in the Letter to the Editor column. Sincerely, Law Office of Dietback, No. 38 Aiduya Road, Wuhe Foreign Firm, No. 21 Yuanmingyuan Road, December 9, 21.

Dear Sir, I have read the news column of your newspaper on the 7th of this month, which stated that the police obstructed the Boy Scouts, and that a police officer with number 2729 from the First Station of the Fifth District even obstructed them because he failed to obtain tickets. After investigating, this office does not have a police officer with that number, and this incident did not occur. Moreover, Baoshan Road is not within the jurisdiction of this office. It is indeed a rumor. Please correct it immediately. Sincerely, First Station of the Fifth District, Shanghai Public Security Bureau, December 9.

Important News of Education

Solid Division of Education Funds in Various Counties of Jiangsu 159

Baozhen, Suxi, Chang Kunyu and other seven counties have already divided the funds. The Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office failed to divide the education funds in various counties properly. The financial bureaus of each county are directly commanded by the provincial departments, and the Education Funds Management Office is not directly under the jurisdiction of Yangzha. Therefore, there is no way to report the funds to the provincial departments first, and the management office is behind, and even the funds are misappropriated. As a result, the counties fail to report the education funds properly, and the education funds in Jiangsu Province are very tight. In order to eliminate this malpractice and seek to ensure the safety of the funds, the office has separated the busy cao under the field tax item of each county and saved it separately, and it is not collected by the county government's financial bureau. A special commissioner is appointed to withdraw the busy cao special funds from the county government's money and grain cabinet and save it separately to avoid misappropriation. At present, the counties that have followed this procedure include Jiangning, Zhenjiang, Wuxian, Wujin, Changshu, Kunshan, and Wuzhuo. The remaining counties are said to be planning to proceed. Yang Zishen and Liu Beihe, section chiefs of the office, are also rushing to various counties to supervise the work of the supervisors sent to urge the payment of education funds in order to collect the funds from various counties, together with the tens of thousands of yuan currently in stock, to distribute the funds to various schools and educational institutions in Jiangsu Province.

Director of Jiangsu Education Department Zhou Fo Hai Inspects Jiangbei Records (5)

County-Established Ruzhong School Address···Visiting Dasheng Textile Factory, Leaving Tongzhou for Shanghai and Then to Beijing 160

Su (Jiangsu) Provincial Education Commissioner Zhou Fohai is scheduled to attend Ruzhou County-Established Middle School at 8:00 AM on the 8th. When the day arrives, [he will] temporarily go to the pavilion, (section chiefs and others will go to various places outside the city and the education experiment area). More than 300 teachers and students of the school warmly welcomed [him], attended a lecture, and were introduced by Principal Xu Xiaochong of the school. The significance of welcoming Commissioner Zhou is not ordinary: firstly, because he is the highest administrative officer of Jiangsu education; secondly, because he is the leader of our youth; and thirdly, because he is a good doctor for diagnosing the problems of Jiangsu education. Zhou took the stage to give an address, briefly mentioning four points: sincerity and diligence. ㈠ Regarding examinations, students should be prepared at all times and should not panic at the last minute. They should be like the military, prepared for wartime in peacetime and calm in wartime as in peacetime. ㈡ Regarding further education, families without the means should not force their children to pursue further education. If further education is difficult, as long as there is usual cultivation, there will be no problem. He briefly described his own experience as proof. ㈢ Regarding employment, the common problems in society today are both overstaffing and a lack of talent. In China today, where all industries are declining, although there are few employment opportunities, if one has rich knowledge and skills, there is no need to worry about not finding a place to succeed. However, one should not hope for too much, and should, as the ancients said, "aim high but start small." ㈣ Regarding moral character, junior high school students are in a period of rapid physiological and psychological change. During this period, if good habits can be formed, life will be beneficial; otherwise, life will be bad. It is hoped that teachers and staff will manage students strictly and not be negligent or mislead people. Students should also manage themselves strictly and not be romantic or self-indulgent. The address lasted for more than an hour, then he returned to his residence, changed to a car, and went to Tongzhou. At 12:00 noon, he arrived at Tangjiazha. He heard about the textile department of Nantong College, and had lunch. From 2:00 PM, he visited the department's practice facilities and inquired about the situation of teaching and training. Because it was a holiday for the Dasheng Textile Factory, the courses of the department are mostly related to practice, so there was no opportunity to inspect the class situation. He then went to Guangsheng Oil Factory to visit the manufacturing of cottonseed oil, and then to private primary schools such as Jingru Junior High School and the Workers' Children's Primary School for inspection. By the time it was 5:00 PM, he went to the general factory of Dasheng Textile Factory. Deputy Factory Manager Zhang Wenqian, auditor Wu Jixian, and others came out to greet him. The factory's industrial guard regiment and the public security bureau's soldiers and police lined up, played music, and saluted with guns. At this time, those who rushed from the city to welcome him, such as County Magistrate Zhang, the heads of the four bureaus, the county party committee, representatives of various educational institutions and groups, and gentry, etc., as well as Haimen County Magistrate Zhang and Education Bureau Director Lu, also rushed from afar. Zhou met them one by one and had a pleasant conversation. At about 6:00 PM, he visited all parts of the general factory in great detail, and praised the factory's achievements and its position in China's textile and economic circles. After dinner, he continued to visit until 10:00 PM before saying goodbye to those who were seeing him off. He took a car to the Yongchao Inn in Lujing Port to wait for a boat. At about 12:00 midnight, he went to Tianshenggang to board the boat to Shanghai and then to Beijing to attend the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee. On this day, Tangjiazha and the area along the way were covered with welcome slogans, and lanterns and flags were hung to express welcome.

The Standards for Primary and Secondary School Curricula Will Be Implemented Starting in the 22nd Year

Textbooks Should Be Edited According to the New Standards and Subject to Review 161

Nanjing, 9th. The Ministry of Education issued a circular to all provincial and municipal education bureaus, stipulating the following measures for implementing the newly promulgated curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools in stages: ㈠ In the 22nd year, all grades of kindergartens and primary schools should strictly follow the newly promulgated curriculum standards for kindergartens and primary schools from the first semester. ㈡ In the 22nd year, the first grade of junior and senior high schools should strictly follow the newly promulgated curriculum standards for secondary schools from the first semester. ㈢ In the second and third grades of junior high schools in the 22nd year, if the arrangement of the teaching material outlines in the new and old curriculum standards of each subject differs too much, the old standards may still be used until graduation, so as to avoid repetition or discontinuity. ㈣ When primary and secondary schools implement the newly promulgated standards, they should immediately adopt textbooks that are edited according to the new standards and reviewed by the Ministry.

Chinese Language 163

First, Objectives

(1) To enable students to understand the inherent culture from the national language and script, so as to cultivate their national spirit.

(2) To develop the skills of using vernacular and language to narrate, reason, express feelings, and convey ideas.

(3) To develop the ability to understand simple classical Chinese.

(4) To cultivate the habit of reading books and the interest in appreciating literature and art. Second, Time Allocation

Each semester accounts for six hours, and the three years total thirty-six hours.

Grade Semester Hours Course Intensive Reading Extensive Reading Guidance Exercises Total Time

1 1 3 2 6

2 3 2 6

2 1 3 2 6

2 3 2 6

3 1 3 2 6

2 3 2 6

Third, Teaching Material Outline

(1) Reading

(1) Intensive Reading ㈠ Standards for Selecting Teaching Materials: (A) Those that conform to the Chinese party-state system and policies; (B) Those that contain the meaning of revitalizing national spirit and improving the current social situation; (C) Those that contain the common knowledge and thoughts that citizens should have without violating the trend of the times; (D) Those that conform to the reality of life and the development of students' physical and mental health without being frivolous, obscene, or passively pessimistic; (E) Those that narrate clearly, reason thoroughly, describe truthfully, and express feelings sincerely; (F) Those that have simple punctuation, harmonious syllables, and no grammatical or logical errors; (G) Those whose style can serve as a model and can promote students' writing skills. ㈡ Arrangement of Teaching Materials: (A) Vernacular and classical Chinese are selected together. The amount of vernacular Chinese decreases and the amount of classical Chinese increases. The proportion of each school year is approximately 7 to 2, 6 to 4, and 5 to 5; (B) The arrangement of various literary styles: in the first year, emphasis is placed on narrative and expressive writing; in the second year, emphasis is placed on explanatory and expressive writing; in the third year, emphasis is placed on argumentative writing and application documents.

(2) Extensive Reading The standards for selecting reading materials, in addition to applying the items listed in Section (1) of Item (1), are briefly listed as follows: (1) Biographies of famous people at home and abroad and systematic historical records; (2) Annotated masterpieces; (3) Ancient sayings and collections of modern speeches; (4) Ancient and modern people's books and letters; (5) Travelogues, diaries, and notes of famous people ancient and modern; (6) Annotated poetry selections; (7) Collections of essays and short stories ancient and modern; (8) Scripts of operas and dramas and valuable works of popular literature and art; (9) Periodicals suitable for students' level.

(2) Essay Writing (Taught During Exercise Time)

(1) Grammar and Syntax (Sentence Patterns, Word Positions, Parts of Speech)

(2) Essay Structure (Selection of Material, Structure, and Descriptive Methods)

Fourth, Summary of Implementation Methods

(1) Reading

(2) Intensive Reading The main points of teaching are as follows: ㈠ Teachers should extract the key points of the writing methods of the selected texts and instruct students so that students can understand the style of the text and its writing methods, and briefly describe the content and the author's life, so that students have a brief understanding of the whole article. The emphasis is on arousing the motivation for self-study, and there is no need to explain word by word and sentence by sentence. ㈡ Students should be instructed to use reference books, such as dictionaries, general dictionaries, encyclopedic dictionaries, biographical and geographical dictionaries, etc., and guide them on how to use them. ㈢ Before the teacher explains, students should first use reference books to check unfamiliar words, difficult sentences, and various questions about people, places, and times. ㈣ Special attention should be paid to explaining unfamiliar or difficult single words and terms encountered in the selected texts. ㈤ After the teacher's explanation, students should be guided to do analytical, comprehensive, and comparative research to ensure thorough understanding, or to raise questions for students to study on their own after class. ㈥ Students should be guided to recite aloud in the national language within the scope of not hindering other people's work to cultivate an interest in appreciating literature and art. ㈦ Students should be instructed to record the key points instructed by the teacher and the results of their self-study in a notebook for reference. ㈧ Achievements should be checked at any time. The methods are as follows: (A) Review, (B) Questions and answers, (C) Tests, (D) Dictation or Recitation, (E) Rotation Reporting and Discussion, (F) Inspection of notes.

(2) Extensive Reading Students are allowed to select books to read according to their individual interests and abilities. In addition to periodicals, at least two types of books should be read each semester. The main points of teaching are as follows: ㈠ Methods should be devised to motivate students to read and to instruct them in various reading methods. ㈡ Questions should be raised about the books students read and they should be instructed to conduct systematic research. ㈢ Reference materials for the books read should be presented. ㈣ Students should be instructed to record the reading methods instructed by the teacher, the answers to the questions, and the key points or questions extracted during self-study in a notebook for reference. ㈤ Attention should be paid to students' recitation, connection, and level of understanding. ㈥ Examinations of achievements should be held periodically or temporarily. The methods are the same as the four items (B), (C), (E), and (F) of the method for examining intensive reading achievements.

(2) Exercise Essay Writing and Composition Exercises Change Teaching Every Other Week. The Main Points Are as Follows:

(1) Essay Writing ㈠ Appropriate materials should be adopted to allow students to study freely in advance so that they can be explained and discussed in the classroom on a regular basis. ㈡ The examples used must be linked and compared with the intensive reading text so that students can get sufficient practice and understanding. ㈢ Examples of grammatical and structural errors in students' exercises should be pointed out and they should be instructed to correct them. ㈣ Attention should be paid to the comparison of vernacular grammar and classical Chinese grammar and the similarities and differences of various styles.

(2) Composition Exercises ㈠ Teaching composition methods should be varied from time to time. A few examples are listed below: (A) Topic selection: The teacher assigns the topic or the students select it themselves and the teacher determines it. The topic should be taken from real life and emphasis should be placed on narrative description, and it should be closely related to the style of the intensive reading text. (B) Translation: Translate classical Chinese into vernacular, or translate ancient poems into vernacular prose. (C) Organize materials: The teacher provides fragmented materials and instructs students to create a systematic text. (D) Change the complexity of the text: show concise text and instruct students to deduce the original meaning, or show lengthy text and instruct them to abbreviate it. (E) Sketching: Divide students into several groups, the teacher prompts them with objects and they actually describe them. (F) Notes: Notes from classroom lectures and extracurricular reading. (G) Records: Records such as diaries, travelogues, speeches, and news. (H) Application documents: Exercises in letters, deeds, regulations, advertisements, and common official document formats. (2) Each exercise must have individual or joint criticism, corrections, or various symbols should be added first so that they can be modified by themselves. (3) Oral practice is carried out outside of class, or the teacher assigns a topic and instructs students to give a speech, or the students freely express their opinions, or a debate is organized and divided into groups for debate. After the speech or debate, the errors in their national language, grammar, and theory should be criticized and corrected. (4) In addition to briefly explaining penmanship and structure in class, attention should be paid to extracurricular practice and copying of regular script. The first requirement is neatness, followed by beauty. Notebooks and composition books can also be used as data for examining calligraphy achievements.

Disaster-Stricken Students Get Free Tuition 165

Nanjing, 9th. On the 9th, the Ministry of Education stipulated measures for waiving tuition fees for students from disaster-stricken provinces. Students who request free tuition due to serious disasters in their place of origin, except for the three northeastern provinces which have been ordered to proceed and the famous counties in Jiangxi Province that have suffered from bandit disasters, which will be handled separately, must first submit a report from the county and city governments of their place of origin to verify the actual situation. A letter should be sent directly to each school for review. Those in national schools should have their tuition and miscellaneous fees reduced as appropriate. Those in provincial and private schools should have their tuition fees reduced as appropriate. Students from bandit-stricken counties should be exempt from all tuition and miscellaneous fees. For counties that are seriously or slightly affected by bandit disasters, national schools should have their tuition and miscellaneous fees reduced as appropriate, and provincial and private schools should have their tuition fees reduced as appropriate. This is limited to this year.

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Schools

Students Whose Parents Have Left Shanghai Are Ordered to Withdraw 172

Those who have already left Shanghai will not be allowed to re-enroll in the fall.

The schools established by the Shanghai Municipal Council have never enrolled children from outside Shanghai, that is, those who reside in Shanghai but are not taxpayers in the Public Concession, and their children must also pay an additional quarter of the tuition fee. The Education Committee decided at the last meeting that from now on, these affiliated students must be admitted only when there is a surplus of children of taxpayers in the concession. It was also found that there are 33 Western children and 32 Chinese children in the Council's schools whose parents have already left Shanghai. After consideration by the committee, these students should be ordered to withdraw from school in accordance with the regulations. However, it is easier for Chinese children to transfer schools and there are fewer difficulties, while if Western children are ordered to withdraw from school, there may be more difficulties, especially those who have reached the graduation level. However, since the Council's schools are maintained by the taxpayers' donations and tuition fees, there should be a fair way to do things. Therefore, it was resolved that: (1) Children whose parents have already left Shanghai will not be allowed to re-enroll after June 1933, and those with special circumstances should report to the Education Committee for special consideration. (2) In the future, if parents of students leave Shanghai, their children should be ordered to withdraw from school immediately. This resolution was submitted to the Board of Directors on the 7th for consideration and approval.

Patriotic Speech Contest for Elementary School Students 173

(The competition and evaluation methods have been announced by the Municipal Party Department yesterday)

The Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department, in order to stimulate the patriotic thinking of elementary school students and develop their speech talents, has organized a patriotic speech contest for elementary school students, which has been announced. All elementary schools in the city will start reporting today (the 10th). The competition method and evaluation method are excerpted as follows:

Speech Competition Method ㈠ This method is based on Article 6 of the Competition Rules. ㈡ The Party Department will consult with the Education Bureau to issue a circular to municipal and registered private elementary schools to comply with the Competition Rules. ㈢ The Party Department will publish a notice in the newspaper informing the schools to report to the Party Department within the registration period. ㈣ The Competition Rules and registration forms will be printed by the Party Department and sent to the Education Bureau for distribution. ㈤ The Party Department will send letters to solicit prizes and invite judges. ㈥ The Propaganda Section will handle the registration, arrange the venue, prepare the prizes, arrange the procedures, and other matters that should be handled. ㈦ The Party Department will announce the results of the finals and issue prizes immediately. ㈧ The evaluation criteria are as follows: (A) Thought and curriculum: 40%; (B) Tone and attitude: 40%; (C) National language and actions: 20%. ㈨ The evaluation form will be formulated by the Propaganda Section and distributed to the judges. Detailed methods will be determined separately. ㈩ This method will be implemented with the approval of the Standing Committee.

Competition Evaluation Method ㈠ This method is based on the provisions of Articles 8 and 9 of the Competition Method. ㈡ One chairman will be set up among the judges to be responsible for compiling and verifying scores and reporting the results, who will be specially invited by the Party Department. ㈢ Each judge will have a notebook for recording scores, which will be distributed by the Propaganda Section. ㈣ The judge's seats will be arranged in rows and will not be concentrated in one place, nor will they be given any other markings. ㈤ The results and rankings of the competition will be determined by the chairman based on the score records of each judge, and then averaging the scores, with the consent of all the judges. ㈥ The results of the finals will be notified by the Party Department temporarily. ㈦ This method will be implemented after review by the Standing Committee.

The Training Headquarters Sends Personnel to Inspect the Fudan Student Volunteer Army 176

In order to promote military training in various schools, the Training Headquarters specially sent personnel to various schools to inspect and examine the results. This morning, they went to inspect the Fudan University Student Volunteer Army. When Major Chen Bingchang, the inspecting officer, arrived at the school, the students had already lined up in formation, a total of four battalions, and the band conductor Chen Wude. Chests full of medals were directing back and forth, extremely busy. Instructor Guo Jian coordinated everything. At 10:00, Lin [missing character], Chairman of the School Military Commission, and Zhang Yifei led the inspecting officer to the venue. After each battalion saluted as usual and inspected the formation, the performance began. The combined platoon training was commanded by Wu Zhaisen, the first battalion commander and a graduate of the former 19th Route Army's Follow-up Training Class. The students marched neatly and were full of spirit. The fierce north wind made their vigor even more evident, and the inspecting officer nodded in approval. After the performance, the military exercise was changed to weapon exercises, performed by the second battalion. First, there were various basic exercises, and then there were trench charges and bayonet drills. The sound of gunfire and shouts of killing shook the ears, and the onlookers even suspected that they were on the front line. After various military exercises, the inspecting officer gave a speech, saying that the Fudan student volunteer army was training conscientiously and moving sensitively, but there were still some small actions that had not been paid attention to. However, judging from today's results, it is truly the champion of all schools, and it is truly an honor for your school. Regarding the issue of issuing firearms, it is currently not possible to issue them immediately. It is necessary to observe the achievements of each school and whether the authorities of each school can be responsible. The Training Headquarters is planning to develop and rectify military training in various schools, and will have the instructors of each school directly commanded by the Headquarters. However, the Headquarters is feeling extremely short of funds, and it is feared that it will be difficult to realize it for a while.

New Broadcasting Information on Family Education Lectures 179

Originally, the Great East Book Company's Family Education Lecture scheduled for yesterday was to feature Professor Zhang Yaoxiang of Jinan University speaking on "Children's Psychological Problems." However, due to other engagements, Mr. Zhang was replaced by Mr. Meng Shouchun, editor-in-chief of the Great East Book Company, who spoke on "A Comparison of Chinese and American Families." His speech briefly stated: I studied in the United States for eight years. Besides studying academically, I also paid attention to their family situations, so I could offer a reference for improving Chinese families after returning to China. Now, let's start with the organizational structure. American families have a small organizational structure, while Chinese families have a large organizational structure. Therefore, their family organization is unusually simple. However, they tend to live with the mother-in-law rather than be supported by parents. This is because there cannot be two mistresses in a family. The mother-in-law can still listen to the orders of the aunt, but the young mistress finds it difficult to listen to the orders of the old lady. Conflicts between daughters-in-law and mothers-in-law are thus eliminated. This is also a characteristic of American families, so I often call American families matrilineal, while Chinese families are patrilineal. In addition, there are various comparisons in terms of economics, morality, marriage, etc., which are extremely interesting. Due to space limitations, I cannot record them all. It is said that today Zhang Yaoxiang will change to speak on "The Lives of Children in Our Country."

Mr. Bao Jiusi Returns Home After Completing His Studies 182

Mr. Bao Jiusi, a native of Yin County, Zhejiang Province, went to the United States at his own expense in 1928 and entered Whittier College. In the summer of 1931, he obtained a Bachelor of Arts degree. Later, he enrolled in Northwestern University to study social economics. This summer, he was awarded a Master's degree from the university. Mr. Bao returned to China via Canada last month and arrived last Wednesday. He has now been hired by the board of directors of the Shanghai YMCA to serve as an executive officer.

丨Rebound of Five Taels and Nine Qian丨

(Breaks Above the 800 Taels Mark Again) After days of successive declines, the benchmark gold price showed signs of rebounding yesterday, breaking through the 800 taels mark again with rapid momentum. However, the volume was limited and the fluctuations were relatively calm, with a range of only four taels or so throughout the day. Overall, it rose by five taels and eight qian. Sentiment was strong. The silver market saw a decline in British prices and stable American prices, but the forward rates fell. The exchange rate saw a rise in British rates and a fall in American rates. The gold price initially rose sharply because of this. Finally, news was heard that France may repay war debts, and the gold price was pulled back to the 800 taels mark. Here is a record of the market conditions before and after.
