Bond Prices Plunge by Around Two Yuan 201

(Market Sentiment Weak, Decline Sharpest, Trading Exceeds 11.3 Million)

Yesterday (the 9th), the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange saw sparse spot transactions; futures trading was brisk with prices falling. Upon investigation, bond prices opened weak at the start of the morning, reflecting market sentiment and large holders engaging in disposals. Scattered sales were smooth, leading to a general decline in prices, ranging from several fractional amounts to over one yuan. During the mid-session, the market showed some buying interest, causing prices to fluctuate. The afternoon opening saw no major changes initially, but buying momentum picked up, leading to a continued decline. The closing session saw the sharpest drop, reaching around one yuan, due to dwindling buying interest and persistent selling pressure. Consequently, aside from the minimal fluctuation of the 96 Financial Bonds, the Sixth Consolidated and Customs & Disbandment bonds each dropped by a little over one yuan, while others fell by a significant amount, ranging from 1.67 to 2.5 yuan. It is said that the sudden drop in bond prices is due to the approaching year-end and the increasingly pessimistic outlook on diplomatic relations with Japan, making the overall environment less favorable. The total value of spot transactions for the day was only 20,000 yuan, while futures trading amounted to 5.17 million in the morning and over 6.1 million in the afternoon, totaling 11.33 million yuan.

Manufacturers Replenish Near-Month Cotton 204

The cotton market remains firm, but the US cotton government estimates that production has increased by another 780,000 bales. This quantity is quite alarming, but market prices have not been affected, so the people in this port are also calm as usual. The extreme shortage of spot goods is also a major factor. A certain manufacturer released a large amount, and in view of the decline in sources from all sides, will replenish the near months, and the market is tight. However, the decline of Indian cotton is uncertain, but it is temporarily difficult to get close to the Shanghai market.

(Zheng Biao Good Qian Half) At the opening of Zheng Biao's previous market, although US cotton increased, its decline was not large, and the gold market rose, and the public sentiment was still stable. Moreover, sellers replenished, and each month rose by one and a half qian. The situation remained hard at the afternoon opening, and each month was flat, with a 5-fen rise in the distance. The total transaction volume for the day was 28,700 dan, and the sales included Yuanda at 2,300 dan, Ruidai at 1,800 dan, Chang at 3,100 dan, and Mingde at 1,500 dan. Purchases included Xincheng at 5,000 dan, Shenji at 1,000 dan, Qingfeng at 2,100 dan, Zhenda at 1,000 dan, and Yiyu at 800 dan. The closing prices are listed below.

US Cotton Government Report 205

Another Increase of 780,000 Bales

Washington, 8th: The sixth cotton harvest estimate in the US was officially released by the Department of Agriculture's Statistical Bureau today, with a production of 12,727,000 bales, an increase of 780,000 bales from the previous estimate. The situation for the same period in the previous six years is listed below (in thousands):

Grain 207

Rice Market Situation Improving

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, sources at West Road decreased slightly, about 50-odd boats. City shops had better appetite than the previous market. Yang Du Jian was sold as soon as it arrived, and the price was firm by about 1 jiao. Su Tong Bang and Changxi North Japonica were all raised by 1 jiao and a half. Early and late rice, Jin and Guang's two groups were handled, and the price was also tight, changing to shade and the yuan to selling well or poorly. The situation is downstream.

(New Zha) Yesterday, only 32 rice boats from Changxi and Xianzizi, and other groups under Suzhou River arrived. Trading was flat in the morning, but in the afternoon, a telegram from Changshu said that the market for brown japonica was improving and the public was excited. Northern Japonica and Bo Dao rose by more than 1 jiao, and Yang Du Jian and Yuan Yuan were stable.

Rumors of Taiwan Rice Being Dumped in Tianjin 208

Three Batches of Near and Far Term Transactions | Price 9 Yuan 3, 4, 5 Jiao

According to news from Tianjin, Japanese merchants in Tianjin are trying their best to sell flour, wheat, and rice in the market. Both flour and wheat have considerable transactions. Australian flour and wheat, handled by Japanese merchants, are priced 5 fen less than those of British and American merchants, or even close to money. At present, the local flour and wheat have fully satisfied their appetite. It is heard that Jiangnan white rice will be transported north, and Taiwanese rice in stock is being sold at a discount. A small amount of Taiwanese rice was transported to Tianjin for trial sales the day before yesterday, which was very suitable for the local foodies. However, the asking price was around 11 yuan, but now the price has been reduced, and a batch of near and far terms has been negotiated and loaded. Spot goods are 9.5 yuan in Tianjin currency, near-term is 9.4 yuan, and delivery next year is only 9.3 yuan. Therefore, the Tianjin rice market has been affected, and the white Japonica, which once sold as high as 13.5 yuan, has gradually dropped to close to 12 yuan. According to this statement, there are also rumors in the rice industry, but Tianjin grain merchants have not admitted it. Whether it is true or not, I think there will be facts to prove it soon.

Biao Flour in Equilibrium 209

(Manufacturers Limit Prices and Sell a Small Amount)

Yesterday, the flour market was generally stable in the morning for each month. Foreign wheat quotations fluctuated very little, and manufacturers generally remained cautiously selling few. Foreigners' sentiments were slightly active, so each month was slightly better than the previous day by about 5 li. Until the afternoon, when the market opened, trading was slightly smooth. It was heard that the Fu and Gao factories had limited prices for sales, and there were a few sales in March, April, and May. Because the market rumored that there were military actions in Shanhaiguan, and the Tianjin gang had received private telegrams, people's minds were inevitably more empty. However, manufacturers quoted prices for transactions, and the quantity was not large. As for foreign wheat, there was no fixed price yesterday. However, for Australian wheat loaded on a ship in January, the foreign firm was willing to sell at 3.25 yuan, but the manufacturer had to change it to February, which was not achieved. As a result, this month was slightly better than the previous day by 2.5 li, January was slightly worse by 2.5 li, February was unchanged, March was slightly worse by 2.5 li, and May was slightly worse by 5 li.

Wheat Futures Quiet 210

Yesterday, the wheat futures market was generally stable in the morning and afternoon for each month. Foreign wheat quotations did not fluctuate much, so both buyers and sellers were calm. However, the sale of foreign wheat continued, and people were inevitably worried. Although the current wheat crop is not abundant, foreign wheat can be used for delivery. At present, it is heard that there are two or three ships of chips on the industry's side, and they are waiting for an opportunity to cash out, so the situation in the future is ultimately easy to be controlled by foreign wheat. Each market transaction only fluctuated by 1 fen, and the results were all the same.

New Sugar Price, Green Arrived, Lack of Price Increase 212

(London Forward Sugar Returned Down 1 Shilling 75)

Yesterday, a telegram from New York on the 8th said that spot sugar prices rose slightly to 8.75 cents, and futures for December were unchanged at 1.359 cents per pound. July was higher by 2 pounds. Also, on the same day, a telegram from London said that December fell half a penny to 5 shillings and 4 pence, March was down 1 shilling and 75 pence to 5 shillings and 6.75 pence, May was down 1 shilling and 75 pence to 5 shillings and 8.50 pence. Also, Java white sugar remained at 8 shillings and 3 pence, unchanged. As for the sugar market in this port, the gold salt saw a good return, but the sales remained sluggish. The association's allocation trend remained the same. High-quality 24 coarse sand white was allocated at 15 taels and 4 qian, with a few transactions. The substitute currency was called at 15 taels and 3 qian and a half, but no allocation was seen. However, it was heard that a dark allocation of 3 qian had been made the night before, so yesterday's entrants only dared to bid this price, resulting in no transaction. Xin Chaoqing borrowed 90 packages yesterday, and opened at 9 taels and 2 qian and a half to 3 qian immediately, which was better than before by 2 qian. The Capture of Square Fort (3) 237

— French Mériel's Photographic Translation

We followed the assault team, running forward: The Russian soldiers suddenly let out three shouts, three distinct shouts, then fell silent, not firing a shot.

"I don't like this silence," the company commander said; "it's not a good sign at all."

I felt our soldiers were too noisy, and I couldn't help but secretly compare their chaotic shouts with the enemy's solemn silence.

We quickly reached the foot of Square Fort. The barricades had been destroyed by our shells, and the ground churned up. The soldiers, shouting "Long live the Emperor," jumped over the new ruins and broken walls, their shouts even louder than the countless times they had shouted before.

I raised my eyes, and I will never forget what I saw. Most of the smoke had risen, hanging like a canopy twenty feet above Square Fort. Through the bluish haze, we could see the Russian soldiers behind their half-collapsed fortress, raising their weapons, as still as statues. I can still see each soldier with his left eye fixed on us, his right eye hidden by the gun he was holding up. A few steps away from us, beside a cannon's muzzle, a man stood with a lit torch in his hand.

I trembled all over, thinking my last moment had come.

"Alright, the dance is about to begin, goodnight!" my company commander shouted.

These were the last words I heard him utter.

A drum roll came from inside Square Fort. I saw all the guns tilting. I closed my eyes, and I heard a hateful explosion followed by shouts and groans. I opened my eyes, and I was surprised to find myself still alive. Square Fort was once again enveloped in smoke. Around me were wounded and dead bodies. My company commander lay face down at my feet: his head blown to pieces by a shell, I was covered in his brains and blood. Only six soldiers and I were left alive in our company.

Following this massacre was a moment of shock. The regimental commander, with his hat on the end of his sword, was the first to climb the fortress, shouting "Long live the Emperor!" Immediately, everyone who was alive followed him up. I can hardly remember what happened next. I don't know how we ran into Square Fort. The two sides fought hand-to-hand in the thick smoke where nothing could be seen. I believe I must have killed someone with my saber, because it was covered in blood. Finally, I heard someone shout; "Victory!" The smoke gradually cleared, and I saw blood and corpses covering the soil of Square Fort. The cannons were all buried under piles of corpses. About two hundred men, wearing French uniforms, gathered together in a confused state, some loading their guns, others wiping their bayonets. Standing with them were eleven Russian prisoners.

The regimental commander lay bleeding on a broken ammunition box near the entrance to the battery. Several soldiers rushed to surround him; I went closer.

"Where is the oldest company commander?" he asked a sergeant.

The sergeant shrugged his shoulders with a very expressive look.

"What about the oldest lieutenant?"

"Well, this gentleman arrived yesterday," the sergeant said in a very calm voice.

The regimental commander smiled bitterly.

"Well then, sir, you are in command now; please quickly have the entrance to Square Fort fortified with wagons, because the enemy still has the strength to attack; but General C will come to help you." he said to me.

"Regimental commander, are you badly wounded?" I asked him.

"Ah... dear, but Square Fort has been captured!"

Translated in Paris, Winter 1931

"Patriotic Lottery Tickets" 238

— Liu

Yesterday, this newspaper reported that the Shanghai Local Association sent a letter to the Municipal Government, requesting that the issuance of so-called "Patriotic Lottery Tickets" be stopped. A gentleman said: This is not only "disappointing," but it is simply like "forbidding patriotism!"

Originally, since last year's September 18th Incident, when the Japanese boldly created the so-called "national crisis" for us, "national crisis" and "patriotism" immediately became the most fashionable slogans on our lips. At first, the public cried for the "national crisis" and paraded to demonstrate "patriotism." As a result, Nanjing was often crowded with "patriotic men," and the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum was especially soaked with a lot of "tragic tears." After a while, the public felt that tears were ultimately limited, and that parades and demonstrations were inevitably too strenuous. Thus, "crying" changed to "shouting," "Long-term resistance!" "Armed recovery of lost territories!" This way, shouts spread throughout the country! After a longer period of time, the public again felt that there were many ways to save the country. It was true that one did not have so many tears to cry all the time, and it was also a bit exhausting to keep shouting all the time. As long as we maintained a bit of sincerity and never forgot, then where would we not be suitable? And the way of "long-term resistance" was precisely contained within this. As the saying goes, "Know it mysteriously and understand it clearly, it exists in the person." Once this thought was turned around, all worries were dispelled. As a result, "crying" stopped and "shouting" ceased. Everyone put on the nonchalant air of a great power. Those who played cards could play eight rounds of "national crisis" cards, and those who danced might as well dance a few rounds of "national crisis" dances. As for "marriages during the national crisis" and "birthday celebrations during the national crisis," these were even more grand and justified. In any case, as long as "national crisis" or "patriotism" was linked to things like "playing cards" and "dancing," then the way of "patriotism" was exhausted, and a heart that was always "bittersweet in joy" could also be seen by all. By extension, if we had money, we might as well go to enjoy "nation-saving" "entertainment." If we had talent, we might as well "save the nation through entertainment," because these were all great avenues to save the country. As for simply taking out money to donate to the volunteer army fighting the Japanese soldiers in the frozen lands of the Northeast, or impulsively rising up and actually joining the volunteer army to fight the Japanese head-on, those were all fools and idiots!

Since the public was all so "patriotic" and "nation-saving," then the issuance of "Patriotic Lottery Tickets" was not simply following the trend of the times, walking the great road of "patriotism." And the Local Association actually did not allow the patriotic lottery tickets to be "patriotic," so the gentleman again said: "To err is human; is that not so?"

Crossroads of Time and Love 239

— Zhang Ziping

Shuhua smiled in a very interesting way after speaking.

"It's cold here, let's go to the classroom to talk."

Haiquan was never willing to delay time because of meaningless talk.

"Okay. Let's go inside. Class is starting soon."

Shuhua responded to Haiquan.

"Don't you come to our sacred classroom!"

"Who wants to go to your zoo with stale air!... Doesn't understand anything, just shits every day, buys that shit!"

Shuhua twitched her nose at the short man, then, with a flick of her left high-heeled shoe, she turned around, and the hem of her coat drew a semicircle, touching the hem of Haiquan's cotton robe.

"Sorry."

She suddenly smiled at him again.

"It's okay."

He replied, while thinking that touching a part of her coat was already a "stroke of good luck," so why was she apologizing to himself.

"Shouldn't have that idea!"

He quickly suppressed the overflowing emotions, while also recalling the situation when he accidentally shook hands with Mrs. Hezi while watching a movie last night. He thought,

"Men are always loving."

The three of them walked through the mountain path of the campus and arrived at the left entrance of the main building.

Another gust of north wind sweeping dense yellow dust rushed towards them from behind the main building. They quickly went inside. Their classroom was downstairs. Ms. Zhuo's classroom was on the third floor.

"It's going to snow soon."

She said, and with one hand on the railing, stepped on a few steps of the ladder.

The two of them walked into the science classroom. Indeed, as soon as they entered from the outside, they smelled a stale odor. Most of the students had arrived. Some were sitting and reading newspapers, some were copying notes, some were standing by the window daydreaming, and some were standing on the podium, writing large characters on the blackboard with half a chalk.

"The weather is particularly cold early this year."

"Damn it! They charge us so much tuition, and the classroom doesn't even have a stove."

"It's so cold. I really don't want to take notes."

"Demand handouts!"

"Agree! With handouts, you don't even have to go to class."

"Old Wang, that would be great. With handouts, you'd still be sleeping in bed at this hour, right? Haha, haha!"

"What does Old Li equal to?"

One student asked a student sitting in front of him, holding a notebook.

"One four one four one two two"

A Study of Cursing 240

— Zou Zou

A German once told me that cursing is most developed in Germany, and that there had even been a dictionary of cursing published. After listening, I secretly thought that this crown might not be worn by the Germans. Although education is not widespread in China, the art of cursing is very widespread. Illiterate village women are all doctors of cursing. If the cursing words from all over China were collected, they would definitely become a very, very large dictionary. Now let me classify and discuss the origins and uses of cursing words. In general, the purpose of cursing is to make the cursed person feel unpleasant emotions. Under this general purpose, various methods have arisen. ㈠ The saying goes, "Humans are the spirit of all things," and mankind has always respected itself and despised animals other than humans. Therefore, curses such as "beast," "pig," and "raised by a dog" have arisen. ㈡ China is a Confucian country, especially worshipping ancestors. Moreover, because it is a male-centered society, sexual intercourse has always been regarded as something that men initiate and women passively receive, as if the initiator is benefiting and the receiver is at a disadvantage. Therefore, curses such as "fuck your mother" and "fuck your ancestors" have arisen. When women curse people by saying "fuck your mother," it is nothing more than wanting to regard themselves as the initiator. In Susong, Zhejiang, there is the curse "fuck your father," which can be explained by this. This kind of curse is the opposite of extreme respect for Confucianism, so it is limited to China. ㈢ Because of the emphasis on men and the devaluing of women, women's reproductive organs are regarded as extremely dirty and lowly things, so when cursing women, curses such as "stinky cunt" and "cheap cunt" have arisen. ㈣ Pointing out the cursed person's dishonorable places to shame him, such as "pockmarked face" and "lame three." ㈤ Death is what everyone dislikes, and unusual ways of dying are even more disliked. Therefore, curses such as "beheaded," "thousand cuts," "little ghost," and "beheading ghost" have arisen. ㈥ Cursing words are originally words of emotion, so they are often transformed and used as interjections, becoming the speaker's catchphrase. For example, when people in Guangdong speak to each other: "Sir, damn that mother, yesterday I went out, damn that mother..." and so on, too numerous to mention.

The Sisters I Cherish 241

— Ms. Biyao

The sisters we don't know are all those we encounter when we go out, and the sisters we do know are also countless; however, the ones that are carved deepest in our hearts are only a few for each person. The few in my heart do not necessarily have particularly deep feelings for me, but rather their unfortunate backgrounds, each representing a type of person, make me feel touched when I encounter that type of archetype, and then I think of that one sister. Although life is wandering and uncertain, the images of these few sisters are deeply rooted in my heart, constantly drawing out the flowers of memory, making people feel lost and unable to control themselves.

1. Suffering Yahong

Before the age of seventeen or eighteen, Yahong was truly what was called "lotus-like face and willow-like eyebrows." Her father feared that her beautiful face would bring her a short life, so he gave her this name. But in fact, the roots of a short life had already been planted at that time. In the thoughts of the late Qing Dynasty, as long as a woman lived a long life and married a husband to grow old with, that would be a great blessing; as for whether their spiritual condition was compatible, that was irrelevant. She was born with a husband, no, she was summoned because there was already such a marriage contract concluded in the world. When she was born, her betrothed husband was riding a bamboo horse in the yard! When that boy was seven or eight years old, he suffered a serious illness. When he fully recovered, he lost most of his intelligence and became a semi-idiot. Later, they studied in the same school, Yahong was a leader in Class A, and he was at the bottom of Class D. This was in the Xuantong era, when male and female students did not communicate when they met; however, mischievous boys often wrote sentences such as "A face red like a melon and a winter melon reflecting each other" on the blackboard before class. "Winter melon" meant fool. Yahong would always hang her head and shed tears when she saw it. In the sixth and seventh years of the Republic of China, she graduated from the normal school department. At that time, it was the era of absolutely virtuous mothers and good wives education, and feudal moral virginity concepts still permeated the world of educated women. Under these circumstances, Yahong had no other option but to be sad. When the wedding date arrived, she resigned from her teaching position and quietly returned, as if she were a little lamb going to the Taimiao Temple to be sacrificed, obediently being carried away by flowers and sedans. For more than ten years since then, she had suffered the abuse of her unreasonable husband, not allowed to read books or newspapers, not allowed to serve in society. She was only allowed to be idle in a lifeless, inactive home. Sometimes, if she slightly went against his wishes, he would use his fists and feet; Yahong would just grit her teeth and resign herself to fate. Recently, her plump and moderate figure was said to have become as thin as dry firewood, and she often coughed up bright red blood.

2. Mad Baixian

Baixian was a talented woman in the early days of women's education. She struggled with her poor and helpless situation, graduated from a normal school in the country, and then went abroad to enroll in a university. Whenever overseas students gathered to discuss the problems of their motherland, one could often hear her passionate discussions. But since the thirteenth and fourteenth years of the Republic of China, her traces had disappeared. It turned out that the tide of love-supremacy had swept her into another world. She did not sink into sweet illusions, but rather became isolated from the crowd. The women's association she founded locally suffered a major blow because of this, with sighs of "If this person does not come out, what will happen to the association's affairs?" After several years, news suddenly came that she had failed in love, became a nun three times, and attempted suicide twice. Recently, a friend from Anhui said that her perception had been completely disordered, and she was only being protected by her relatives, living in a temple on a famous mountain. The changes in life are so dramatic! Recalling her initial departure abroad, how many aspirations she had for social issues—especially for women's issues—but now she was half-foolish and half-dazed, worse than the deer in the mountains! If her spirit could regain her previous clarity for just a moment, and she was told that someone had lost their entire soul for love, I think she would definitely have a reasonable evaluation. Who can not regret that she was too emotional and lacked reason when dealing with her own problems?

Futurist Dancing 242

— Juquan

Dancing is the expression of mankind's harmonious movements, and primitive humans already possessed this instinct. In ancient savage tribes, after successful hunts or victories in war, there was a kind of dancing to express joy. Later, as culture advanced, dancing became a kind of art. During the Renaissance, Medici promoted the art of dancing, and so dancing became very popular from then on. Now, in Europe, the most popular is the waltz. The waltz is a dance style of moving forward and backward, using three-beat music. The great musicians Johann and Strauso had specially composed for the waltz, so it was quite popular in European dance halls for a time.

Before the Great War, South American dances were popular in Paris, such as the Brazilian "Maxine" dance, the Argentine "Tango" dance, and the Paraguayan "Santate" dance, which some people called impressionist dances. Later, Cubism rose up, making dancing an independent art. Before, dancing was infused with music, but the new dance separated from music and occupied an independent position.

Now what we are going to talk about is Futurist dancing. Italian Futurist artists Marinetti and others recently published a Futurist dance (La Danse Futuriste) manifesto, advocating the application of the principles of Futurist art to dancing. In his manifesto, he begins by talking about the historical path of dance art. In primitive times, mankind's unknowable and immeasurable terror of the universe was expressed in dancing. Therefore, the dancing of savages mostly imitated celestial phenomena—the rotation of the sun and moon, the movement of stars. Later, as human culture advanced, dancing was gradually able to express the spontaneous movements of the human body. Futurism is vigorously praising material civilization, and mechanical movements are the elements of material civilization, so Futurism believes that what civilized people's dances should imitate is this kind of movement. Also, for the view of music, Futurism's claims are very unique. They believe that the music that has been used in the past is a kind of sick state of art, and the music used by Futurist dancing should not be music, but "noise"—the "noise" made by vibrating solid objects, liquids, or compressed gases. Because only this noise can express mankind's mechanical life. Futurist artist Luigi Rusoro invented instruments for making noise based on this principle for use in dancing.

Now let's give an example of a Futurist dance advocated by Marinetti. There is a kind of dance called Aviation, which is a dance that simulates the movements of aviation. A map of the earth is laid on the ground. Above it is hung a blue curtain, representing the sky. The dancers wear a propeller on their chest and a model of a monoplane on their heads. While dancing, they report the altitude of the flight, "Three hundred meters... five hundred meters..." Green mountain scenery is also placed on the stage, and the dancers must jump over the mountains. When dancing, the specially made instruments emit the sounds of storms. Sometimes electricity is even used to release electric sparks in the room to represent lightning.

In short, the main purpose of Futurist art methods is to oppose everything that is inherited. The dance art of the past was characterized by gentleness, harmony, evenness, and tranquility. Futurist dancing, on the other hand, takes violence, reversal, and agitation as its main purpose. Although this kind of dance is not very popular in continental Europe, and the general public does not welcome it very much, and there are many attacks, Futurism has clearly established a new style in various modern arts.

Republic of China, Year 21, December 10th, Saturday (No Extra Cost)

Handwritten Report by Dr. Zang Boyong 245

Definitely the Best Among Chicken Juices

Solving Three Difficulties of Winter Supplementation 255

By Zhang Ruwei

We work diligently throughout the year, depleting our essence and blood. Timely supplementation during the winter is an essential way to nourish life. However, there are three difficulties in choosing supplements, detailed below. I will also provide solutions based on my research, one by one, as follows.

Supplements are Often Greasy and Cause Many Problems

All kinds of supplements are often greasy. Taking them can cause stomach upset, constipation, and indigestion. The benefits are not seen, but the harms are numerous. Moreover, their tastes are bitter and astringent, and their smells are especially difficult to bear. For example, donkey-hide gelatin and yellow-lipped fish liver oil have a particularly fishy and foul odor that is difficult to approach. All are unpalatable, and the spleen and stomach easily stop digesting. However, "chicken extract" or "beef extract" provides sufficient nourishment and tastes palatable. Taking it increases appetite and has no drawbacks. It is most suitable for those who want to supplement but are afraid of taking medications.

Too Many Supplementation Procedures are Discouraging

There are too many procedures involved in various supplements: selection, purchase, distinguishing authenticity, matching ingredients, decoction, timely consumption, consulting a doctor, or daily injections. It is time-consuming and laborious, and the effects are very slow. This causes people to become discouraged and lack perseverance. As a result, they stop halfway, and no effects are seen in many cases. However, "chicken extract" and "beef extract" have been researched and produced under medical supervision. Taking them is convenient and requires no procedures.

Taking Too Much Supplementation Can Be Harmful

Taking supplements requires a specific daily dosage. If too much is taken, it is not only useless but will inevitably cause many drawbacks. For example, if someone has anemia and takes too many blood-tonifying products, it can turn into a congestion syndrome, making them prone to stroke and other conditions. However, "chicken extract" and "beef extract" have been researched by the medical community and are prescribed to be taken at one bottle per day. Its tonifying power is appropriate for the daily needs of one person.

Talks

A Romance Case 271

— Meicun

Every day, when I open the newspaper and look at the local news, I always find one or two articles about romance cases. Newspapers try their best to reveal these cases, so that people in society can be aware and not repeat the mistakes. Although romance is romantic, it always feels like an attention grab if it goes to court. Is it a business tactic? Even though imprisonment is for a limited term, the taste never feels as delicious as fish and meat. But because it is limited, risk-takers may want to try it out.

The characters in romance cases can be young or old. Recently, there was a news story about a 31-year-old unmarried woman who went to Suzhou to marry her lover. As a result, her father followed her to Suzhou and sued her husband in court for fraudulent marriage. There was another story about a Sichuan broker, so-and-so, who seduced a girl under the age of 16 and was sentenced to three years and six months in prison. They are all young guys in the stories. The plots of the affairs are ingenious in their own way. One has already been sentenced, and the other is still being resolved. It is not pretty to drag romantic friends into court.

If you want to be attractive, if you know what's good for you, then just go to Xizang Road (near the racecourse) or Route des Soeurs (near the Great World) to open your eyes. On the black-and-white signs hanging horizontally and vertically, you can recognize some saviors of romantic diseases. Then you can carry out your romance cases that can avoid litigation, which is relatively worthwhile. But then again, doing so is attractive, knowing what's good for you, and also considering the adults and gentlemen. It doesn't lose what they call personality. But not like this, you just have to watch the old actors perform last year. How meticulous his old man's layout, handsome and sensible, can take care of, but also grand, although it has caused a lot of newspaper criticism, but there is no imprisonment in court. Some say that with money and power, everything can be perfunctory? I think so too!

The affair between a country and another country can also be a warning. However, it's somewhat unreliable to have the League of Nations as our only judging court. It is clear that it is unreliable, but it is given to it to solve, only because of the magic of the other side's propaganda and power. The most appropriate expedient is to wait.

Finally, we must be grateful to the romantic young man who "does not love the country but loves the beauty" for creating such a major romantic karma.

1

If you were born with some strength, you wouldn’t obtain a privileged athlete in school. 2

So morning exercises became the most hated thing by students, but too much absence is very important for future graduation, then just ask someone to come on behalf of you, or make excuses for illness. The discerning physical education teacher will never investigate.

5

I did a small statistic. That is, when Mr. × is giving a philosophy lesson, there are an average of thirteen "ha" sounds per minute when he is lecturing.

6

There is a theorem in arithmetic that A + B = C. I think it can be changed into the most contemporary thing, that is, (love) + (leather) = death. Let me explain it: that is, two people love each other plus a leather coat, or leather wine. To put it harshly, it is a "flesh relationship", and finally the two commit suicide.

7

If students constantly pull out their watches to check the time during class, it is enough to show that the teacher is not humorous or cannot attract students' attention.

8

It is extremely difficult for students who are generally young masters and princes to concentrate on their studies. If you ask him what day of the week "Christmas" and "New Year's Day" are, and how many days off there are in school, they will definitely know.

9

Whenever there is a lecture in our school, if the person standing on the stage and gesticulating is a blonde, blue-eyed foreigner, then the stage will be as quiet as if there were no one there. But it's very different when we have a memorial week. There are fights, eating, reading novels… In short, it's a feast for the eyes.

10

I heard that a few days ago, a celebrity at sea held a ×× anniversary, and a certain important person sent a plaque. The cost of "porterage" alone was 5,000 yuan. I don't know how much was donated to the Northeast Volunteer Army?

Store Clerk Communications

How to Get Another Opportunity to Study 275

Dear Editor:

I am an unfortunate person who has not received a complete education, a young man who is about to finish his apprenticeship. Since graduating from high school, my aspirations and my father's expectations were to continue to junior high, high school, and university, but the aristocracy of our country's education system, the economic downturn, and all kinds of environmental pressures everywhere caused my aspirations to study to encounter various obstacles. So in the end I had to take the path of dropping out of school. After dropping out of school, I sought help from relatives and friends to seek employment outside. About a few months later, thanks to the kindness of my relatives, I was recommended to learn the oil business in my county. After entering the store, I became terrified of my lack of knowledge; moreover, this company was established for about a year, and due to sluggish business and huge expenses, it closed down.丨Middle omitted丨

Later, after many twists and turns, I was loved by my closest relative who had recommended me earlier and asked me to work as an assistant accountant in his cotton yarn shop. It has been a year now, and I am still in his shop, waiting for a good opportunity. However, the precious time of our young people is passing by like an arrow leaving the string丨Knowledge has not progressed at all, how can we not sigh丨However, how can I get another opportunity to study in the future; satisfy my desire for knowledge; and embark on the path of light, but I am at a loss. Just when I was frowning, I suddenly saw your newspaper's sixtieth anniversary, and you specially opened the store clerk communication column to answer difficult questions for employees and apprentices in the industrial and commercial sectors. I don't dare to be presumptuous. I beg you to give me some wise advice.

Sincerely, Zhu Jinlin, December 6th

Editor's Note: It is truly the most painful thing in the world to have a very high desire for knowledge and not be satisfied. Zhu Jun's vexation is a natural phenomenon. However, in China today, under the conditions of this social economy on the verge of bankruptcy and the education system being so unsound, we are only discussing Shanghai, and I don't know how many tens of thousands of young people are in the same situation as Zhu Jun. Therefore, Zhu Jun's letter is specially published for discussion. In addition to offering a little bit of foolishness, I also hope that readers will actively participate and give opinions.

First: We feel that it is certainly best to be able to go to school to study, but if the environment does not allow it and there is no such opportunity, you can also study without going to school, because learning is a lifelong career, and books are as vast as the sea of smoke. If you rely solely on school, how much can you actually read? | Furthermore, there are many shortcomings in the current schools. Not to mention those that are poorly equipped or have a business flavor; even those that are better in the results have limited real benefits to students. Diligent students, graduating from college, at most only know the method of reading and the doorway of learning. If you want to achieve profound achievements, you still have to continue to work hard after graduation. How can you get it completely in school?

Second: If you want to have sufficient knowledge and increase your knowledge, it is certainly necessary to read; but books are just symbols that record people's thoughts and experiences or describe various things, and are not the "panacea" for solving all problems. If you don't have a good observation of society and a good understanding of things, just reading books will not only not help your knowledge, but will often make you more and more confused. The so-called "good readers can increase their wisdom, bad readers can increase their ignorance," is the reason. What's more, the universe is originally a book that encompasses everything, and there are still many things that have not been recorded artificially. If you rely solely on books to seek everything, then your mind will be too narrow.

The above two points seem too transcendent, but in reality, if we are willing to take a closer look, it is also very common sense. Zhu Jun has been confused by the arguments of ordinary people, which has led to extreme vexation: In my opinion, Zhu Jun's environment is not bad and there are many opportunities for self-study. Being an assistant accountant is much better than an ordinary apprentice. You may wish to devote one or two hours each day in your spare time to specialize in reading. Over the years, knowledge will increase invisibly. If you encounter something you don't understand, you can humbly ask others for advice. No one will not tell you. If you do this, although the progress is slow, if you can persevere and not fall into the problem of being hot for three days and cold for four days, you will eventually succeed one day.

Finally, I also hope that Zhu Jun and friends who have the same feelings as Zhu Jun will not be too pessimistic about the environment they are in now. You must know that there are many great philosophers or great writers in the world who have not received a full school education but have been successful. This is certainly related to special talents, but most of it is completely struggled out of difficulties.

But we deeply feel the universality of this problem, and hope that readers will express their opinions, which will be published in this column one after another. Now I will write this question again below: "How can store clerks, apprentices, or interns satisfy their desire for knowledge?"

Submission Guidelines for the Amateur Weekly of This Newspaper 277

This newspaper publishes an amateur weekly every Sunday. The submission guidelines are as follows:

1. This journal is named Amateur Weekly. Submissions of the following types are welcome:

(1) Methods for improving amateur life: (entertainment, sports, self-cultivation, etc.)

(2) Store clerk, worker, apprentice, etc., self-description of life; (e.g., my interest and opinions on the business)

(3) Literary works depicting the lives of store clerks, workers, apprentices, etc.;

(4) Scientific management methods for industry and commerce;

(5) Talks on industrial and commercial ethics;

(6) Common sense of industry and commerce;

(7) Life or interview records of industrial and commercial leaders;

(8) Small business management methods;

(9) Other interesting essays about the industrial and commercial world.

2. The style of writing is not limited, but it should be clear and vivid.

3. Submissions must be written clearly, preferably with modern punctuation.

4. The author's name will be signed when the submission is published; but the true name and detailed address must be indicated at the end of the manuscript; and a seal must be added for verification when receiving payment.

5. The editor has the right to delete or modify submissions; those who do not wish to do so must declare in advance.

6. Submissions will not be returned whether or not they are published; however, this rule does not apply to lengthy articles of more than 2,000 words that are declared in advance and accompanied by return postage. 7. Once a submission is published, the copyright belongs to this newspaper.

7. Once a submission is published, the remuneration will be generous; if it is found that it is a plagiarism of someone else's work, or has been published elsewhere, the remuneration will be cancelled immediately. 8. Please send submissions directly to the Amateur Weekly Society of Shen Bao.

Fiction

Writing a Letter to a Friend's Wife (Continued-3) 278

— Tai Shou'ou

You might readily say that I am not spirited, but rather cruel and murderous. It is likely that the training my stepmother gave me was too special. From the moment I understood how to read, I knew how to fight to the death. I don't understand what things are worth cherishing. At any time and any place, I am always prepared to use my strength and blood to fight to the death with any enemy that is unfavorable to me or unsatisfactory to me. … Let me tell you more clearly: don't be afraid! Several times, I almost fought Dajing to the death because of the impulse of anger!

There is another story that I can tell you in passing, but, my dear little Pig Luo, don't have nightmares tonight!

At that time, I was still a very comfortable university student at Kou University. One early summer evening, a sudden commotion arose in the dormitory. The reason for the commotion was that our classmate Hong Shiguang had been beaten and injured. Hong Shiguang was a Jiangbei person with whom I had absolutely no emotional connection. His beating, just like someone dying on the street, was not enough to attract my attention, let alone elicit sympathy or comfort.

"This is truly outrageous! Hong Shiguang went to a certain car company as a customer to hire a car. Just because of one sentence, he offended their accountant, and was beaten so badly by more than a dozen car drivers! His right eye probably cannot be saved!"

"That certain car company relies on a foreign merchant's brand, so it's not easy to sue!"

The students spread and discussed the incident of Hong Shiguang's beating, as if it were news from society, gradually arousing my murderous intent. "Matters that cannot be remedied by law can only be resolved by fighting to the death." On one Saturday night, harboring this idea that did not shy away from the stench of bloodshed, I filled myself with old wine and hid a sharp short axe. Without taking a car, I found a certain car company on foot. The weather was hot at the time, and a group of rogue-like car drivers, all with different arrogant airs, gathered at the entrance of the car company to cool off. No one would have noticed me.

"Aiya!" A big, burly shoulder was the first to come into contact with my sharp axe. Seeing that I came fiercely, they all raised benches, bamboo brooms, and wooden sticks, and surrounded me. There were at least twenty strong men. I acted as if I didn't see them, didn't say a word, and like a mad tiger, I just chose the places where there were many people to chop and ram, my fists and elbows, benches, crashed on my body, more powerless than paper, I simply didn't feel any pain.

The shouts of killing alarmed the street patrolmen, who rushed in to mediate. The other side immediately abandoned their armor and stopped fighting, while my sharp axe was still flying in the wide car park.

Partly relying on the imposing manner of the suit I was wearing, and partly thanks to the drunken state that reddened my face, the two patrolmen not only did not send me to the Western prison in Tilanqiao, but also carefully helped me, called a rickshaw for me, and sent me off with great respect.

As soon as I got into the car, I was very proud. I rubbed my empty hands together, secretly celebrating the victory tonight. The car pulled halfway, and the night wind slowly woke me up: head, shoulders, legs... there was no place without alarm bells, it turned out that I was covered in wounds! In the end, I also discovered my weapon, the sharp axe, had been confiscated by the police officers.

Three months of lonely illness on a sickbed in Baolong Hospital was the result of this "seeing injustice on the road and drawing a knife to help." Hong Shiguang never knew about this.

Savage? Children! Cruel? To be honest, I myself have not failed to realize it, but I can't change it!

Thank God! All thanks to him for giving me this blood that is brave to fight to the death, so that today, I can finally endure the pain of infinite sacrifice, voluntarily give up you, the you that is on my mind day and night, abandon a promising future, move my old father and orphans, and my most pitiful wife, and go alone to face the muzzle of my enemy that I have hated for more than ten years - the Japanese beast army!

If anyone is arrogant enough to place the titles of "patriot" or "martyr" under my name, then I can only be ashamed and cannot accept it. Because this time I am abandoning my pen to join the army and devote myself to the country is, undeniably, to preserve your reputation and happiness. Sacrificing for the country is just a way to embellish the posthumous glory! Therefore, you don't have to pity me, or be sad about it, just enjoy all the material pleasures that your Dajing offers you!

On the day I left, a day when it was raining heavily, the idea of seeking death was decided. At lunchtime, I specially changed into the newest suit that you thought was the most beautiful, and carefully tied a bright tie. After carefully shaving my beard, I poured and combed it with a type of hair oil with the strongest fragrance, and combed the two rows of hair as flat as if they were drawn in black ink. After dressing up so comfortably, I lingered in front of the mirror of the wardrobe for a while. "I really don't know which lucky bullet will end the life of such a handsome and outstanding young man!" I suddenly had a whimsical idea, and very happily thought to myself.

Overseas News

Recent News of Lillian Gish 279

— Jianan

Movie fans who have watched movies for three or four years will not forget Lillian Gish, who is known for her tragic roles in Hollywood. She doesn't have the beauty of Billie Dove, the sweetness of Nancy Carroll, the heat of Clara Bow, nor the mystery of Garbo, but when the films she stars in are screened in any theater, they are always full to the brim and a sensation. In her previous silent films such as "Broken Blossoms," "The Scarlet Letter," and "The Wind," her silent, tragic, posture and expression have earned the sympathetic tears of many men and women. But since the advent of sound films, her fame seems to have been blown clean by Vitaphone. She is not like Chaplin, who opposes sound films, nor is it because her voice is not good, because she had a very successful performance in the stage play "Uncle Vanya" performed in New York. Recently, in the sound film "Romantic Nights," which was screened at the Shanghai Grand Theater, she also received considerable praise. Her temporary return to the field was originally due to dissatisfaction with the conditions set by the bosses. It is said that in the contract with MGM, she asked for a weekly salary of $8,000, which the company did not agree to, so she turned her head and returned to her hometown.

After years of hard work, she has some savings. There is no need to worry about future life. But she never forgets her love for the art of drama. She often studies facial expressions, simple movements, and correct postures in front of the mirror. In addition to socializing in the local social circles, she often accepts theater appointments to perform on stage. This is not a reaction to the end of the road, but an opportunity for her to develop her personality and maintain her glory.

Recently, she also performed "Camille" in Central City, Colorado. It is a famous French work, which has been introduced to us twice in films by Valentino and Ramon Novarro. This time, relying on Lillian Gish's talent and experience, her success on stage is certain.

As a result of this, the old bosses in Hollywood are jealous again. Contract negotiations are brewing again, and perhaps both parties will compromise a little. Let's prepare to welcome her.

Movie Review

"Downstairs" Movie Review 280

— Jie

John Gilbert has almost lost all his former glory since the popularity of sound films. "His Glorious Night" was a sound film, but not only was the sound not welcome, but his performance skills seemed to be inferior to the silent era. He hoped to restore his reputation, so he first wrote a novel, assuming himself to be the protagonist in the book. Sure enough, Americans had a much better impression of him. After that novel was made into this film "Downstairs," he almost regained his former status.

"Downstairs" is being screened at the Carlton. We who usually love him, of course, want to see what is going on, but unfortunately, he can't give us the satisfaction we imagined!

John carefully changed his style. The character he played is not the amorous and gentle gentleman of the past. He plays a treacherous and unrighteous servant. This point may be considered a success, because he is very suitable for his role and can fully express the personality of a bad man who disguises and deceives women. His vicious inner heart and kind appearance make people understand what he is doing now. His better plan is to use second-rate actors for all the supporting roles and put all the important performances on himself. In this way, a very long film has become his solo performance, and of course it is much easier to please people.

The plot is very tense, and it is also very reasonable and realistic. The structure of the film can also be regarded as acceptable. The photography helped John a lot with his wonderful performances. The light is a bit too dark overall. Perhaps he did it on purpose to describe the "downstairs"?

The supporting roles are all good. Paul Lukas can even steal the show in some places. The two female roles are very mediocre. If the play is acted as a play, it will naturally be overdone or reveal falsehood. Many people on the cast list only appear for a few hundred feet in the film, so there is nothing to talk about.

This time, what is satisfactory is the sound, which has made earth-shattering progress compared to John's previous sound films.

In short, the silent John gave us a very good impression. We have too high hopes for his sound films. Otherwise, if this film were starred by someone else, it could be regarded as a masterpiece, which could satisfy us very much!

"Kismet," originally named "Fate and Luck," but later renamed "Golden Dream," is now being screened at the Cathay. The content describes the naked palace in a vivid and thorough way. The grandeur of the setting is especially amazing. The picture below is one of them.

Film Industry Knowledge

Research on Tone Deafness 281

— He

Tone deafness can make movie stars not recognize their own voices on the screen. This is why many male and female stars are surprised when they first hear the sound coming out of the film.

"My voice sounds very unnatural," or "This doesn't sound like my voice at all." It is said that when Paramount previewed "Blonde Venus," the male lead of this film, Herbert Marshall, did not recognize his own voice. Although he had filmed several sound films, he said that he always felt unaccustomed to hearing the sound coming out of the film.

At the same time, Broadway stage star and Genevieve Tobin's sister, Vivian Tobin, also had such an experience. She is now playing a Roman prostitute named Dacia in Cecil B. DeMille's film "The Sign of the Cross." When she previewed the film, she heard her voice coming out of the film for the first time. She said, "If this voice is supposed to be my own voice, I really can't believe it myself." But the people in the screening room said that her voice was very accurate.

Hansen, the head of Paramount's sound department, gave the following explanation for this contradiction:

"Almost everyone is somewhat tone deaf to his or her own voice." When talking, he hears his own voice through a kind of body vibration and eardrum vibration, but the voice he hears from the film only has eardrum vibration and no body vibration.

John Gilbert's masterpiece "Downstairs" is being screened at the Carlton starting yesterday. This play was originally conceived by Gilbert himself, and there are many wonderful things in it. The picture below is one of the scenes.

Reader Opinions

Talking about "Old Hatred and New Sorrow" 282

— Ailian

The debut work "Old Hatred and New Sorrow" of the three pillars of the Star Company - Li Pingqian, Ai Xia, and Sun Min - is indeed much more satisfactory than the previous products of the Star Company. The script is very well written, and there are also commendable points in the directing techniques.

Synopsis: A young military officer has a love affair with his uncle's concubine. Later, the young man leaves alone and wanders for eighteen years. One day he looks back and returns to his uncle's house, but the concubine has already died. He still lives in the old house and teaches his cousin earnestly. Unexpectedly, the cousin's love buds bloom, and he is extremely painful and has no choice but to pretend to be crazy, forcing his cousin to transfer her love to another young man.

Director: Li Pingqian's skill is not weak and far better than the old-fashioned people like Zheng Zhengqiu. For example, the beginning is the young man's debauchery in the ballroom, and then a photo reminds him of the old things of eighteen years ago, and then a train is conjured from a letter, reflecting "Wandering for seventeen years since then" are all unique and always tense.

Actors: Gong Jianong's performance is very profound; Ai Xia first plays the uncle's concubine, which is very mediocre; later she plays the cousin, which is just right. Sun Min plays another young man, which is a bit of a waste of talent. Zhu Qiushui is still suitable for his role. The subtitles are half good and half bad. The music composed by the Central Orchestra is not bad.

Conclusion: In today's domestic films, it can be regarded as a masterpiece. I would like to ask everyone to watch it out of enthusiasm for maintaining domestic films.

Film Monograph

Crying Without Breathing Help 283

— Chen Dabei

After laughing, we are now going to cry.

Crying is easier than laughing. We can cry when we are first born. Is it still necessary to spend effort to discuss and practice it?

But if you have a little experience in the photography studio or on the stage, you will definitely know that the expression of crying is more difficult to make than laughing. In a large photography studio, I don't know how much film is wasted every year on this simple expression that everyone can't do. "Miss Zhang! Mr. Li! Those two crying shots of yours have to be reshot tomorrow! Because after printing it out and looking at it, this time it looks like laughter!" This disappointing announcement is often heard even by the most experienced famous stars in the photography studio. Small companies cannot reshoot unsatisfactory shots due to economic constraints. As a result, they have no choice but to cut off a few feet. The most important film in the whole film is just because the protagonist's crying looks like laughter.

Now you first try crying in front of the mirror without breathing help. The first thing that changes naturally is your eyebrows. Many people may think that frowning is crying. This is how crying looks in our old operas.

The second thing that changes is your lips. When crying, the lips often droop, the upper lip stretches slightly downwards, and the lower lip and chin hang down, lengthening the entire face.

The muscles of the face are completely in a crying state. But it still doesn't look like crying. Because your eyes always seem to be smiling there.
